
-----title
丹棱 (出生地)

id='poem_sentence_2_520291'>长沙虽归如不归，阴山亦复归无期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520291'>绛灌通侯延寿死，琵琶休怨汉天子。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520294'>仙人昔尝为酒星，乘兴痛饮乾北溟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520294'>五湖一吸聊解酲，江妃丧魄鳌失灵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520294'>上帝震怒呵出庭，酡然影落秋山青。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520294'>何须荷锸随刘伶，河沙劫填归冥冥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520294'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>，17岁</div><div id='6247bfe8f1d34c1b9e736a9a8709b2e2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　离家赴太学，由水路出川，有文。作品：《南行祭江渎文》<div id='poem_1213195' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213195' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213195?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南行祭江渎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213195")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213195_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213195'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213195'>年月日，西蜀唐某顿首跪拜江渎之灵，慷慨太息而祝曰：仆草莱野夫，愚不知分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213195_comment'></div>不能与田夫野老佣耕南亩，而背书腰剑，假道荆楚，以游大梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213195_comment'></div>乡里亲戚，笑其狂妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213195_comment'></div>兄弟妻孥，泣涕撮挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213195_comment'></div>而击鼓发棹，奋然不顾，其志盖将有所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213195_comment'></div>他日登金门，上玉堂，垂珰珥笔，昂轩峨冠，亦在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213195_comment'></div>荣耀父母，庇荫兄弟，兼济朋友，养活妻子，亦在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213195_comment'></div>安国家，定社稷，立功名，使千万世不氓，亦在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213195_comment'></div>仆之此行，所望大矣，所系重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213195_comment'></div>神之有灵，鉴其所存，为我拘鼋鼍，蛰蛟蜃，鞭逐鲸鲵，俾无惊湍怒涛之恐，此神之阴助力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213195_comment'></div>其他功名富贵，则人所自致，非敢以祈于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213195_comment'></div>尚享！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1213195_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='045eb49be86b4d77a7d8ca1f2d20ded0_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1090')">1088-1090年</a>，18-20岁</div><div id='045eb49be86b4d77a7d8ca1f2d20ded0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年闰十二月二十五日</a>　父亦因疾复作卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　在家居丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　赴东都应试，有诗。作品：《过潼关》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚应试在元祐七年22岁时，是年仍然在家居丧，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span>《赴阙》<div id='poem_520396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520396")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_520396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520396'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520396'>铁衣十万拥胡雏，手释襟喉计亦疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520396'>阃外不闻天子诏，将军未甚读兵书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520396'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_520396_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_520358' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520358' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520358?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520358")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520358_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520358'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520358'>十年餐苜蓿，梦寐长阑干。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520358'>继粟自不饱，朝齑岂辞酸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520358'>虽无汗马劳，几作蠹鱼乾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520358'>自知爬沙手，未办<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作辨）</span>扶摇抟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520358'>此行敢侥倖，政尔求便安。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520358'>恐或得所欲，圣主天地宽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520358_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520358'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_520358_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='765567992293448bb44e0c3cb250ce40_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("765567992293448bb44e0c3cb250ce40");'><span id='765567992293448bb44e0c3cb250ce40_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>，24岁</div><div id='765567992293448bb44e0c3cb250ce40' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　返丹稜，有文，后由丹稜赴任。作品：《祭祖坟文》<div id='poem_1213190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭祖坟文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213190")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213190_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213190'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213190'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213190_comment'></div>昔我先祖，积善累仁，以垂裕于后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213190_comment'></div>皇天福善，笃生我先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213190_comment'></div>夙有淑质，未幼而学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213190_comment'></div>我先祖以考终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213190_comment'></div>惟我先人，丕承厥志，率德履行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213190_comment'></div>令闻令望，风动于四方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213190_comment'></div>匹夫匹妇，罔不知有我先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213190_comment'></div>时命不与，则竟罔有成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213190_comment'></div>至于小子某不肖，惧忝前烈，早夜祗惕畏慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213190_comment'></div>虽荐更多难，则亦罔敢怠荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213190_comment'></div>而禀赋颛蒙，不能承我祖宗之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213190_comment'></div>天子哀其愚，锡以一命，俾俟罪于益昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213190_comment'></div>非某小子能，实惟我祖宗之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213190_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213190_comment'></div>某生不辰，不逮事于祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213190_comment'></div>夙夜恃怙，则犬马之养，罔有所施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213190_comment'></div>惟是勤劳王事，益尽为臣之忠，庶几有裨我祖宗之绪，不至于陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213190_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213190_comment'></div>酒醴荐羞，虽则不腆，以告其区区之心，祖宗其格思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213190_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1213190_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6bf564051379445cb09fffce0dd9f481_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6bf564051379445cb09fffce0dd9f481");'><span id='6bf564051379445cb09fffce0dd9f481_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，51岁</div><div id='6bf564051379445cb09fffce0dd9f481' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年九月</a>　送女至丹稜，顺路一游峨嵋、青城诸山，有文。作品：《答合守程元老书曰》<div id='poem_1213080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答合守程元老手书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213080")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213080'>某顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213080_comment'></div>李元应到泸，出示所赐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213080_comment'></div>伏承暑中动止万福，眷聚无他，良慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213080_comment'></div>某处田野间，亦复自适，不足垂念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213080_comment'></div>但泸南前日小旱，二麦已不偿种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213080_comment'></div>今又甚雨，复忧麻豆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213080_comment'></div>仕进如此，退耕又如此，岂但人力耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213080_comment'></div>妇雅病肺，比老益甚，五月中垂死复活，今幸无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213080_comment'></div>然以此都不成家计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213080_comment'></div>閒居既无过从，而衰晚亦不耐烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213080_comment'></div>逃虚既久，已自成趣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213080_comment'></div>闻人足音，乃更不喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213080_comment'></div>九月间送女到丹棱，因放脚一到峨眉、瓦屋、雾中、青城诸山，至春末可归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213080_comment'></div>向示漆器，今纳二十引去字号：「闻此宽相忆，为邦复好音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213080_comment'></div>人生五马贵，莫受二毛侵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213080_comment'></div>伏幸检收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213080_comment'></div>合阳过客绝少，公帑有馀，日生事想见不多，多亦不劳馀刃，政当薰衣理鬓，努力行乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213080_comment'></div>自厚，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213080_comment'></div>某顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1213080_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
眉山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0211f554f0ab45c8988b6981eac64d7b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0211f554f0ab45c8988b6981eac64d7b");'><span id='0211f554f0ab45c8988b6981eac64d7b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1086')">1084-1086年</a>，14-16岁</div><div id='0211f554f0ab45c8988b6981eac64d7b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　读书于眉山，师从任德翁，深受赏识，有文。作品：《上任德翁序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）将唐庚师从任伯雨时间置于其15岁时，此处存疑，暂依黄鹏所记。）</span><div id='poem_1213122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上任德翁序<span class='inlineComment2'>（时年十五）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213122")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213122'>薛郡任公之教授通义也，士之曳长裾，服方领，抱书束带，优游于泮宫者数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213122_comment'></div>英俊豪杰，往往辈出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213122_comment'></div>有少年书生曰唐某者，诵书不甚多，属文不甚工，碌碌落落，无可称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213122_comment'></div>一日持一轴书，掉三寸舌，草衣麻屦，攘袂登门，危言高论，不顾忌讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213122_comment'></div>公一见而嗟异之，再见而礼貌之，三见而怜恤之，劝戒勤笃，教谕款密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213122_comment'></div>某处之而不能自安，退而咨之于客曰：「公于我厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213122_comment'></div>吾将图报矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213122_comment'></div>吾欲胁肩谄笑，巧言令色，以顺适其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213122_comment'></div>以是报公，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213122_comment'></div>客曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213122_comment'></div>是小人之报也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213122_comment'></div>「吾将抱长剑，挟匕首，有恶声至者，以血溅其襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213122_comment'></div>以是报公，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213122_comment'></div>客曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213122_comment'></div>是侠客之报也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213122_comment'></div>「吾将淬文锋，砺辞锷，庶几超腾奋跃，高飞远举于天下，使天下之人指之曰：『斯人也，出于任公之门』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213122_comment'></div>是以报之，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213122_comment'></div>客曰：「唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213122_comment'></div>是国士之报也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213122_comment'></div>某因书以为序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1213122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1086')">1085-1086年</a>　眉山读书。<br /></div>
-----end

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年二月二十日</a>　母史夫人殁，庚奔丧回乡，离国学。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8b719a9d756043458f603d0b6d9bd163_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>，21岁</div><div id='8b719a9d756043458f603d0b6d9bd163' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年三月</a>　及进士第，有文。作品：《谢及第启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年仍然在家居丧，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。《宋人传记资料索引》称，庚乃元祐六年进士；《宋史·哲宗纪》则称其绍圣元年三月及第，存疑，暂依元祐六年记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢及第启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1091年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213117")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213117'>射策枫宸，已甘退黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213117_comment'></div>第名桂籍，尚获采收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213117_comment'></div>叨被宠荣，惟知感槩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213117_comment'></div>切以文章君子之馀事，忠义天下之大闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213117_comment'></div>国之休戚，不系于文章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213117_comment'></div>士之进退，莫先于忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213117_comment'></div>方天子临轩而策士，岂徒求摛藻之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213117_comment'></div>而诸儒充赋以在庭，盖亦取切时之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213117_comment'></div>欲考终身之节，必观筮仕之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213117_comment'></div>宜有谠言，少裨睿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213117_comment'></div>如某者少不好学，老方读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213117_comment'></div>左右图史者十年，涉猎经传者万卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213117_comment'></div>杜心浸癖，窦性成痴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213117_comment'></div>虽古今成败之原，粗知其略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213117_comment'></div>而篆刻雕虫之学，本非所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213117_comment'></div>妄意拣金，谩来市璞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213117_comment'></div>青天万里，堪嗟蜀道之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213117_comment'></div>白雪一声，难和郢中之曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213117_comment'></div>笙竽异好，水石难投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213117_comment'></div>自知与世不谐，几欲拂衣而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213117_comment'></div>因缘附骥，侥倖化鹏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213117_comment'></div>入瞻天日之光，亲奉丝纶之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213117_comment'></div>周询要务，冀获至言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213117_comment'></div>顾为学之荒疏，愧乎无补；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213117_comment'></div>若与时而高下，诚所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213117_comment'></div>姑尽节以惓惓，宁抱关而碌碌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213117_comment'></div>夫何献白，亦预拾青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213117_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官匠石群材，钧镕众窳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213117_comment'></div>与人而不求备，嘉善而矜不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213117_comment'></div>苟有寸长，未加尺退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213117_comment'></div>谓其辞虽鄙讷，论不将迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213117_comment'></div>弃在边庭，必能裹尸于马革；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213117_comment'></div>置之言路，必能碎首于龙墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213117_comment'></div>薄示甄收，或堪器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1213117_comment'></div>敢不冰霜志操，金石肝肠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1213117_comment'></div>狱讼簿书，岂辞劳于今日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1213117_comment'></div>功名事业，将有望于他年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1213117_comment'></div>庶免小人之归，永为国士之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1213117_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1213117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_520425'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520425'>家世传儒素，平生学古文。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520425_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520425'>三年思故国，一命荷君恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作明君）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520425_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520425_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520425'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520425_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　有诗。作品：《走笔赠仙姑》<div id='poem_520296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>走笔赠仙姑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520296")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520296'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520296'>仙姑八十春秋高，两鬓墨黑无斑毛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520296'>鹿胎冠子青纱袍，神风清峻真仙曹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520296'>人生瞥忽如销膏，是非海里翻波涛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520296'>五斗官米令人劳，安能俛首争锥刀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520296'>愿仙乞我瓢里一丸药，武陵溪上抖擞世俗腥与臊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520296'>不然教我蝉蜕羽化秘诀之一二，海山深处摘取王母千岁不熟之蟠桃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520296'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_520296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在京任宗子博士，逢张商英乞归，作诗与唐庚别，庚次韵。作品：《次张天觉赠韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年仍在凤教授州任上，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_520271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次张天觉见赠韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520271")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520271'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520271'>别公归去养天和，见说清朝士已多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520271'>裙舍登门何处曳，顶缘受记昔曾摩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520271'>几时傅说重调鼎，去岁成汤已解罗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520271'>会引鉴湖为故事，要从英主乞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_520271", 520271, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>三峨</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520271'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　作行状思其父。作品：《唐先生行状》<div id='poem_1213178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐先生行状<span class='inlineComment2'>（代杜蓬州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213178")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213178'>唐先生讳某，字彦通，眉州丹棱县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213178_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，祖讳某，考讳某，俱不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213178_comment'></div>皇考之捐馆也，先生始六岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213178_comment'></div>是时乡人未知官学，先生孤露自奋，卒为名儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213178_comment'></div>其学博而不杂，其制行和而不流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213178_comment'></div>轻财好施，出于自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213178_comment'></div>盖自尧舜三代以来，理乱废兴，典章人物，莫不考论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213178_comment'></div>旁至诸子百家、天文地理、方技医卜之书，莫不通贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213178_comment'></div>其博至于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213178_comment'></div>然特深于经术，著《四经微旨》行于世，而专用春秋名家，为《讲义》三十卷，《辨三传》七卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213178_comment'></div>大抵以《春秋》为无褒，其于传、注取二三策而已，此所以见其不杂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213178_comment'></div>性简易，不作崖检，与乡人处由由然，无贵贱皆得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213178_comment'></div>比其没也，远近闻之，俱出涕叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213178_comment'></div>逮今二十年，思之不忘，其和至于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213178_comment'></div>然议论刚正，无所阿附，负其所蕴，非其友不友，亦以是见恶于不善者，此所以见其不流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213178_comment'></div>平生用财，不问其数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213178_comment'></div>尝至濛阳，其尉丁忧，贫不得去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213178_comment'></div>先生雅不识其人，倾橐赗之，空手而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213178_comment'></div>其好施类皆如此，而未尝有德色，此所以见其自然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213178_comment'></div>自嘉祐、治平间，先生已有盛名，西南学者争宗师之，授经者累数百人，然应进士举反不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213178_comment'></div>益昌龙图阁直学士陆公诜荐之，亦不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213178_comment'></div>浮沉丘园，无复仕进意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213178_comment'></div>熙宁初，罢诗赋，以经义取人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213178_comment'></div>士论喜其必有所合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213178_comment'></div>既而《春秋》不为经，先生亦老矣，始终不偶，蜀人惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213178_comment'></div>然余尝考其行事，以求其用心，则平生所存，良亦可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213178_comment'></div>族本以治产富饶，而先生专业儒士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213178_comment'></div>方以声律进取，而先生独治经，此其志岂为利禄计哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213178_comment'></div>命虽不偶于今，而其书具存，足以传于后世无穷，复何憾焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213178_comment'></div>元祐三年闰十二月二十五日终于家，享年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213178_comment'></div>前娶家氏，再娶史氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213178_comment'></div>男五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213178_comment'></div>女四人，适某，皆士人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213178_comment'></div>孙男四人，孙女二人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1213178_comment'></div>卜以崇宁三年二月二十八日，葬县之南二十里鼓面山之原，以史氏祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1213178_comment'></div>予顷出守咸安，道过阆中，而先生之子某适宰是邑，倾盖如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1213178_comment'></div>遂定为忘年友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1213178_comment'></div>然则状先生行义以告于士大夫者，非其职耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1213178_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1213178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　是年有水灾，作诗二首记之。作品：《戊子大水二首》<div id='poem_520341' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520341' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520341?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊子大水二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520341")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520341_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520341'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520341'>踏歌喧喧杂铙鼓，潭边呼龙令作雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520341'>龙嗔挥水十大馀，千村万落几为鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520341'>寄谢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_520341", 520341, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>龙神</span>且安处，熟睡深潭不惊汝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520341_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520341'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_520341_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_520342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520342?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520342'>夜半传呼河入室，揽衣下床深没膝<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作床深没下膝）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520342'>旧来水不到谯门，老巫归咎西门君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520342'>西门君去老巫舞，明年却娶河伯妇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520342'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_520342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在京为蔡京作谢启。作品：《谢蔡太师启》<div id='poem_1213091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢蔡太师启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213091")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213091'>始缘力请，得返弊庐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213091_comment'></div>终赖仁私，尽还旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213091_comment'></div>岂惟铭佩，亦复兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213091_comment'></div>某屏迹累年，无识面者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213091_comment'></div>阖门度日，将终身焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213091_comment'></div>自收老大之心，遂绝进升之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213091_comment'></div>未甘扶杖，起居虽健于管宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213091_comment'></div>久已饰巾，志意自同于陈实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213091_comment'></div>忽奉昭回之迹，大推霶霈之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213091_comment'></div>旧恶宿愆，一时荡涤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213091_comment'></div>前侯故将，以次甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213091_comment'></div>顾惟朽钝之躯，屡费陶镕之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213091_comment'></div>终蒙记录，不忍弃捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213091_comment'></div>谓其尝任宰司，故优其班序；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213091_comment'></div>谓其久安田里，仍处以虚閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213091_comment'></div>就使自为之谋，想亦不过如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213091_comment'></div>静循其本，敢不知归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213091_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官以王佐之才，值圣人之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213091_comment'></div>将令四海，尽蒙比屋之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213091_comment'></div>肯使一夫，独掩向隅之泣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213091_comment'></div>致兹衰退，亦极宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213091_comment'></div>食既愈浮，宁有小言之补；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213091_comment'></div>位非所称，得无大耋之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213091_comment'></div>辞受之间，莫知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213091_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1213091_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在京任宗子博士，访韩愈《进学解》作赋，抒发牢骚并自嘲。作品：《归欤赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年仍在凤教授州任上，有诗《苏时中惠茶》，有文《上席侍郎书》，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>归欤赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213063")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213063'>归欤先生，归欤先生！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213063_comment'></div>坐讲六籍，立谈百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213063_comment'></div>突姬、孔之堂奥，刳轲、雄之心髓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213063_comment'></div>游说天子，间关千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213063_comment'></div>射策万言，捭阖乱理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213063_comment'></div>葩吐奇，霞散绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213063_comment'></div>拔犀渠，擢象齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213063_comment'></div>曾不能八事为律，片言寤旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213063_comment'></div>伛偻一命，摧折委靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213063_comment'></div>穷骐骥于捕鼠，困干将于补履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213063_comment'></div>血鹏而肉鲸兮，尚不能逞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213063_comment'></div>刀机之残湿兮，又何足舐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213063_comment'></div>昔薛丞相置东閤以观士，朱游拂衣而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213063_comment'></div>奚扁舟之不汎，岂洞庭之无水？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213063_comment'></div>先生笑曰：「呜呼，噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213063_comment'></div>子言小哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213063_comment'></div>病者嗜于土炭，饿者甘于糠秕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213063_comment'></div>醉者安于遇虎，怒者恬于染指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213063_comment'></div>万法非实，皆由心起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213063_comment'></div>狐尾见于疑目，牛斗闻于病耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213063_comment'></div>宿瘤何恶，颦眉何美？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213063_comment'></div>狐裘何荣，牛衣何耻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213063_comment'></div>吾谓戴安道破琴而不肯作，未若宋之逊秉笏而唱吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213063_comment'></div>阎立本沮气于画师，未若祢正平遗形于鼓史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213063_comment'></div>抱关击柝兮亦悠悠，弹冠结绶兮亦悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213063_comment'></div>吾忘情于彼此者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1213063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　作文表自强不息之志。作品：《次斋铭》<div id='poem_1213171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又次斋铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213171")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1213171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213171'>生而知之，自诚而明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1213171'>学而知之，自明而诚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1213171'>困而学之，又其次者。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1213171'>困而不学，民斯为下。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1213171'>吾少也狂，自以为健。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1213171'>出而接物，然后知困。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1213171'>今虽老矣，幸其未衰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1213171'>陈书于斋，以学以思。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1213171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1213171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1213171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　友人还乡，作诗有感。作品：《友人还乡有感》<div id='poem_520329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>友人还乡有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520329")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520329'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520329'>饥乌哑哑枝上啼，秋风萧萧吹客衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520329'>儒冠误身不得归，女痴妻寒病乳<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作且）</span>老<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作儿病饥）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520329'>归来聚首贫亦好，我固知之归不早。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520329'>束书十载游长安，一官远谢医卜贤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520329'>托生长镵直<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、滚滚作真）</span>可怜，今君别我还故里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520329'>想见亲朋问所以，为言憔悴京尘里。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520329_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520329'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_520329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年三月</a>　为外家史子深作墓志铭。作品：《史子深墓志铭》<div id='poem_1213186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史子深墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观三年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213186")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213186'>君讳通，字子深，姓史氏，世为眉之青神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213186_comment'></div>少与其兄珣，皆以文学知名于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213186_comment'></div>年十七以贡举不中，遂退居于楠溪之上，杜门著书，绝人事者数年，得《易书》若干卷，《乾坤别解》三卷，《礼记义》一卷，《详说》四卷，《律吕气数》十二卷，《书义》八卷，《诗义》若干卷，《论语》、《孟子》解各若干卷，《子史论》若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213186_comment'></div>其书既出，学者翕然称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213186_comment'></div>或曰：「是知古矣，其于时事，未必知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213186_comment'></div>已而君至京师，进《世要机务》十卷，《刍荛策》二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213186_comment'></div>其言当世便利，殆非草茅布衣之士所能言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213186_comment'></div>至于论兵，则虽谋臣宿将，练习边事者，不能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213186_comment'></div>或曰：「是能言矣，其于行事，未必能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213186_comment'></div>已而君起家尉通川，遂能使人畏己，遇事辄断，号为强明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213186_comment'></div>至作磐石令，则又专务宽厚和易，抚字劝课，如古循吏所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213186_comment'></div>盖二邑之俗不同，故君所以应之者亦异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213186_comment'></div>名声大著，诸公交章荐之，而君已卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213186_comment'></div>县人哭泣悲思，至今父老犹喜道当时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213186_comment'></div>吾尝谓学者所贵乎知经者以其能知道，所贵乎知道者以其能应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213186_comment'></div>白首穷经而不能应物，又何以经为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213186_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213186_comment'></div>君学足以知经，道足以应世，而晚得一命，年止五十七，不得以充其志，官止于一县令，不得以尽其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213186_comment'></div>故其应物者，止于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213186_comment'></div>此吾党之士所以嗟惋叹惜为之请铭以葬，而吾亦不得而辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213186_comment'></div>史氏系出鲁国，后徙杜陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213186_comment'></div>唐末入蜀，遂家于眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213186_comment'></div>曾祖、祖、考皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213186_comment'></div>君中元祐三年进士第，历达州通川尉、资州磐石令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213186_comment'></div>年月日卒于官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213186_comment'></div>先娶侯氏，再娶程氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213186_comment'></div>男二人，曰纪、曰彦时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213186_comment'></div>女五人，长适某，次适某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213186_comment'></div>孙男二人，女一人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213186_comment'></div>以大观三年三月日葬于某山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213186_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1213186'>子深之书，学者多有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213186_comment'></div>虽不铭之，自足以久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213186_comment'></div>既足以久，而又铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213186_comment'></div>子深之传，愈久不疑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1213186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_520213'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520213_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　携弟与友人游九龙池，作诗记本年春游。作品：《大观四年春，吾与友人任景初，舍弟端孺自自蜀来京师至长安，时方寒食，吾三人相与戎服，游九龙池，饮酒赋诗，乐甚。是岁吾迁岭表，明年景初亦谪江左，忽忽数岁，皆未得去。寒食无几，念之凄然。作诗寄任，因命舍弟同赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称此诗作于政和三年寒食之时，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_520214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大观四年春吾与友人任景初舍弟端孺自蜀来京师至长安时方寒食吾三人相与戎服游九龙池饮酒赋诗乐甚是岁吾迁岭表明年景初亦谪江左忽忽数岁皆未得去寒食无几念念<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作之）</span>悽然作诗寄任因命舍弟同赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520214")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520214'>居今行古任定祖，底事迁延亦未归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520214'>我坐力田伤地脉，君缘搜句漏天机。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520214'>故都回首三寒食，新岁经<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作惊）</span>心两湿衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520214'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_520214", 520214, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>学道</span>一生凡几化，不因到此始知非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520214'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年六月</a>　张商英拜相，作诗以志庆。作品：《内前行》<div id='poem_520147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520147?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内前行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520147")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520147'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520147'>内前车马拨不开，文德殿下<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作舍人）</span>拜右相，中使押赴文昌台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520147_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520147'>旄头昨夜光照牖，是夕收芒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>如秃帚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520147_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520147'>明日化为<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作朝化作）</span>甘雨来，宅家唤作<span id='poem_sentence_4_520147'>周公礼乐未要<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作制）</span>作，致身姚宋也不恶。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520147_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520147'>向来两翁当国<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>年，民间斗米才<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作三）</span>四钱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520147_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_520147_0'>⑶ 任本作我闻二公拜相，汪本作向来两公拜相</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_520147_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　因张商英荐，提举京畿常平，有文。作品：《诫谕诸路提举常平司恤民》<div id='poem_1213066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诫谕诸路提举常平司恤民</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213066")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213066'>夫理财所以养民，养民所以阜财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213066_comment'></div>知理财而不知恤民，则民且散矣，安得财而理诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213066_comment'></div>财用不足而加赋扰民，其害有甚于是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213066_comment'></div>则财亦不可以不理，此常平之法所以必不可废，虽废而必复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213066_comment'></div>虽然，徒法不能以自行，故国家部置使者任之以权，授之以成，书使专董其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213066_comment'></div>予欲使民仰事俯育，足以自给，汝为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213066_comment'></div>予欲使民凶年饥岁无流离失业，汝恤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213066_comment'></div>予欲使民疾苦呻吟有以自达，汝听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213066_comment'></div>予欲使吏奉法惟谨，无意外凿空以侵渔小民，汝察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213066_comment'></div>庶民艰食，赤子开口，仰哺嗷嗷，吏或恬视，不发圭撮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213066_comment'></div>民所不欲，吏或牵课抑强，以利岁入之赢数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213066_comment'></div>期会未至，吏或文移四出，系累敲扑，以要治办之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213066_comment'></div>汝其纠戒，必罚无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213066_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213066_comment'></div>有弊吏，无弊法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213066_comment'></div>立法之意，至宽至厚，条目至纤至悉，至明至白，汝推行之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213066_comment'></div>无俾民受其害，而归咎于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213066_comment'></div>无俾异意之人得以藉口譊譊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213066_comment'></div>无谓朝廷不汝闻知，朕言维服，其听无怠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1213066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年九月</a>　为张商英所累，遭贬斥，安置惠州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年九月底</a>　有诗记南迁事。作品：《南迁》<div id='poem_520168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南迁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年九月底）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520168")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520168'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520168'>去去宽乡托此踪，闹中无地顿衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520168'>未诛绮语犹轻典，更赐罗浮有底功。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520168'>虾菜贱时皆丙穴，茅柴美处即郫筒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520168'>著鞭要及春前到，趁赋梅花庾岭东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520168_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520168'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520168_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年冬十月</a>　负罪自京南迁，有文记之。作品：《南征赋》<div id='poem_1213059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南征赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年冬十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213059")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213059'>始摄提之孟冬，余负罪而南驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213059_comment'></div>雪盈尺而更繁，风三日而犹吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213059_comment'></div>体冻极而若无，心怖甚而忘悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213059_comment'></div>凡再信而至许，觉惊魂之稍归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213059_comment'></div>访景福之遗基，指空郊之荒泺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213059_comment'></div>曾禾黍之无有，矧栾梁之丹雘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213059_comment'></div>国已挹于三马，臣不闻于一鹗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213059_comment'></div>岂当世之无儒，抑此病之难药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213059_comment'></div>道昆阳而流叹，澹悲风与愁云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213059_comment'></div>阶一夫之僭窃，纷万鬼之烦冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213059_comment'></div>嗟世祖之论功，忘王章之曩言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213059_comment'></div>既直钩之不食，终曲突之无恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213059_comment'></div>过叔子之旧邦，登岘山而痛哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213059_comment'></div>方关右之放贾，盖眼中之拔镞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213059_comment'></div>独何心而表留，卒养痈而溃肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213059_comment'></div>傥遗灵之犹在，当举白而相沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213059_comment'></div>尽荆门之荦确，瞰蜀江之汤汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213059_comment'></div>念故人之久别，觉良晤之甘香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213059_comment'></div>稍回翔于澧浦，忽凌乱于潇湘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213059_comment'></div>时廓舒而浩荡，复收歛而凄凉，味《九歌》之馀哀，闵三闾之孤趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213059_comment'></div>岂公子之足怨，实举国而无与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213059_comment'></div>内不怿于女媭，外见非于渔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213059_comment'></div>持此道以奚归，亦各安于所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213059_comment'></div>自是远矣，行人渐稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213059_comment'></div>水愈激而愈清，山益削而益奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213059_comment'></div>造郴岭之穷处，云湟关之故基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213059_comment'></div>客至此兮返顾，雁至此兮北飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213059_comment'></div>眷武溪之毒淫，吊文渊之矍铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213059_comment'></div>射参狼于陇阪，观跕鸢于浪泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213059_comment'></div>奋身出于万死，誊口喧于百恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213059_comment'></div>信老子之足哀，觉少游之差乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213059_comment'></div>经韶阳而再宿，写石上之遗声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213059_comment'></div>悟圣神之在宥，如天地之生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213059_comment'></div>彼禽鱼固自有理，而日月未尝不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1213059_comment'></div>虽吹万之不同，吾得一而皆正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1213059_comment'></div>舍真阳之短策，放清远之孤舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1213059_comment'></div>觑碧落之灵秘，嘲峡山之媚柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1213059_comment'></div>承悬崖之滴乳，搴袅岸之垂樛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1213059_comment'></div>探羊城于浩茫，发蒲涧于深幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1213059_comment'></div>穷一时之诡观，渺万古之清愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1213059_comment'></div>盖明年之正月矣，始税驾于罗浮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1213059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　途经鄢陵，受知县刘汲之请，作墓志铭。作品：《徐夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1213185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213185")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213185'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213185'>夫人徐氏，其先京兆人，唐末避地，遂家于眉州丹棱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213185_comment'></div>自考以前，蜀人惮远，仕进者尚少，故曾祖某、祖某、考某，三世无食禄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213185_comment'></div>夫人幼颖悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213185_comment'></div>年十二丧所恃，已能顺适继母，无毫发不满意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213185_comment'></div>考为人严重，左右莫敢仰视，独夫人侍侧，辄怡然为之解颜，家人因以白事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213185_comment'></div>年二十归刘氏，舅姑得之喜，即委以家政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213185_comment'></div>方是时，刘氏累世好施，生事萧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213185_comment'></div>夫人既专内事，虽细务必亲之，规画处置，悉有法度可守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213185_comment'></div>未几，刘氏复振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213185_comment'></div>舅姑既没，父母春秋高，嗣子早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213185_comment'></div>夫人奉养丧祭，能尽其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213185_comment'></div>侄有少孤从其母嫁者，夫人取置诸子间，摩顶抚育，无有轻重厚薄，至为婚媾、能自立乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213185_comment'></div>课二子读书甚力，既而二子以次取进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213185_comment'></div>元符三年，长子汲为合州司理参军，奉夫人以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213185_comment'></div>是岁六月二十四日卒，年五十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213185_comment'></div>少子湜登科时，夫人没五年矣，惜乎不及见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213185_comment'></div>汲今以宣德郎知鄢陵县，湜以通仕郎行蜀州晋原尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213185_comment'></div>女适杨某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213185_comment'></div>孙若干，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213185_comment'></div>大观四年十一月日葬于某乡之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213185_comment'></div>其将葬也，鄢陵以行状请铭于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213185_comment'></div>余交鄢陵二十馀年，朋旧之情，既不可违，而夫人之善又不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213185_comment'></div>其事父母舅姑也如此，其治家立门户又如此，收恤孤露而成之又如此，教其子问学、连年取科名、流声号于时又如此，是乌得不铭也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213185_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1213185'>大儿来归，里门下车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213185_comment'></div>小儿来归，拥版以趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213185_comment'></div>官学成矣，系而母且。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213185_comment'></div>而母不留，可悲也夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1213185_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aa5017c9ef104a5bb9a2900b598a82c0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa5017c9ef104a5bb9a2900b598a82c0");'><span id='aa5017c9ef104a5bb9a2900b598a82c0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1120')">1116-1120年</a>，46-50岁</div><div id='aa5017c9ef104a5bb9a2900b598a82c0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　至京后，作祭文怀其父。作品：《焚黄祭文》<div id='poem_1213201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焚黄祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213201")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213201'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213201'>嗣子承议郎某，敢昭告于皇考承事先生、皇妣孺人五十二娘之灵：通籍于朝，逮今十年，遇大礼者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213201_comment'></div>而负罪流落，久隔赠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213201_comment'></div>乃者蒙恩复齿朝著，始赠皇考承事、皇妣孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213201_comment'></div>盖自孤苦垂三十年，然后能取一命以追荣父母，而少伸人子之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213201_comment'></div>其不孝不敏之罪，无所逃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213201_comment'></div>虽善文其过者，莫能为之辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213201_comment'></div>区区之心，考妣其鉴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213201_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1213201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　作诗怀其幼子蜑。作品：《蜑儿歌》<div id='poem_520153' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520153' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520153?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蜑儿歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520153")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520153_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520153'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520153'>泸南二子天一边，思之不见今三年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520153'>阮咸已老得遥集，白发自愧还欣然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520153'>未看颅骨并颊颧<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作头颅并颊颐）</span>，啼中已有过秦篇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520153'>诸田何得贱庶孽，会斩庄贾摧强燕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520153_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520153'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520153_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　上书张商英。作品：《上张观文所业书》<div id='poem_1213081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张观文所业序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213081")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213081'>某惶恐顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213081_comment'></div>某欲焚弃笔研之日久矣，而时时技痒，终不能自制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213081_comment'></div>虽制亦不能久，今日暂止，明日复作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213081_comment'></div>如间日疟，不断根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213081_comment'></div>昨既至惠州，便用赵广汉法为缿筒，每一篇成，辄投之缿中，不可复取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213081_comment'></div>比其还也，始破缿出之，得歌诗杂文三百馀篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213081_comment'></div>念持此无所归，必归之门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213081_comment'></div>而篇目猥多，无气力装写，但写古、律诗百篇，杂文二十篇以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213081_comment'></div>辞既不工，虽工亦安所施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213081_comment'></div>亦各致其所爱习而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213081_comment'></div>隐几一阅，即投之火中，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213081_comment'></div>干冒钧重，悚愧无量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213081_comment'></div>门生具位序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1213081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　为乡人史南寿作墓铭。作品：《史南寿墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称是年立春，唐庚于江陵作诗《和观文相公立春日示诗》，与黄鹏所记是年已至开封异，暂依黄鹏记录。马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称是年唐庚立春位于江陵，溯江西行经宜都，四月过夔，至江津，妾黎氏卒，六月五日至泸州，九月返丹稜，因游峨眉、青城诸山，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史南寿墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213180")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213180'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213180'>邑人史南寿，以政和七年戊戌卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213180_comment'></div>其子卜葬地，得至孝乡善听里山池之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213180_comment'></div>卜葬日，得十年十一月己酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213180_comment'></div>于是遣使来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213180_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1213180'>公之系，太原史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213180_comment'></div>九龄名，南寿字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213180_comment'></div>鼻祖灏，尉临邛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213180_comment'></div>属唐末，不复东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213180_comment'></div>居吾乡，为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213180_comment'></div>自克恭，丹棱令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213180_comment'></div>曾祖珵，祖正辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213180_comment'></div>父大同，世高赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213180_comment'></div>列甲第，名上田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213180_comment'></div>产钜万，僮指千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213180_comment'></div>公少时，习于富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213180_comment'></div>捐金钱，如粪土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213180_comment'></div>朝游谁，韩王孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213180_comment'></div>暮过谁，左阿君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213180_comment'></div>居击钟，出连骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213180_comment'></div>盛而衰，亦其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213180_comment'></div>时既异，事不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213180_comment'></div>客益落，家屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213180_comment'></div>身困约，气不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213180_comment'></div>捧笑腹，伸谈眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213180_comment'></div>里人子，丧所怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213180_comment'></div>尸在地，贫不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213180_comment'></div>公闻之，时方食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213180_comment'></div>弃匕箸，起太息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213180_comment'></div>立解衣，易缗钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213180_comment'></div>税其孤，众翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213180_comment'></div>调棺衾，具饭含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213180_comment'></div>赙毕集，尸乃敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213180_comment'></div>性嗜书，多所藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213180_comment'></div>尤喜医，受禁方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1213180_comment'></div>公为方，殆天得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1213180_comment'></div>诮生桓，起死虢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1213180_comment'></div>欲为书，施无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1213180_comment'></div>草未就，以寿终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1213180_comment'></div>寿几何，七十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1213180_comment'></div>阴种德，莫知数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1213180_comment'></div>德既熟，穫者谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1213180_comment'></div>娶王氏，生两儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1213180_comment'></div>长易简，吾故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1213180_comment'></div>有气节，能苦辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1213180_comment'></div>次行简，尤所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1213180_comment'></div>学已优，时未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1213180_comment'></div>女二人，皆已行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1213180_comment'></div>宋师锡，洎孙京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1213180_comment'></div>孙男一，孙女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1213180_comment'></div>男耆卿，女幼稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1213180_comment'></div>穴故乡，为新坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1213180_comment'></div>近先垄，利后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1213180_comment'></div>中有铭，文百句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1213180_comment'></div>句三言，信万古。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1213180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　侍女黎氏是年方北归还乡，作文记其事。作品：《黎氏权厝铭》<div id='poem_1213183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黎氏权厝铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213183")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213183'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213183'>侍女黎氏，扬越人，八年随吾遵海滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213183_comment'></div>丁酉北归至江津，一疾即死不及伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213183_comment'></div>月实丙午日壬寅，葬之未可携莫因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213183_comment'></div>权厝于此，有子存，何以识之考斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1213183_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　作挽词吊故人。作品：《何执中挽词》<div id='poem_520279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何执中挽词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520279")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520279'>白璧就黄壤，忘情良独难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520279'>观生六十化，比没九迁官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520279'>笔下无时俗，胸中有岁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520279'>雅怀嗟不遂，欲挂死前冠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520279'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在京赋闲，提举上清太平宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年十一月</a>　为亡兄作墓铭。作品：《亡兄墓铭》<div id='poem_1213181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亡兄墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213181")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213181'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213181'>先公奉议，有子五人，兄其长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213181_comment'></div>少时爱书，为文章，治《易》、《春秋》，皆有家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213181_comment'></div>其志岂易量哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213181_comment'></div>已而病肺，不得尽其力以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213181_comment'></div>然天资孝友，所立有绝人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213181_comment'></div>正使力学，其得亦不过如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213181_comment'></div>元祐三年秋，先公游泸南，予兄弟持母丧于丹山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213181_comment'></div>兄夜半蹴予曰：「吾梦收尊书，发之得『亟来』二字，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213181_comment'></div>尊得无他乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213181_comment'></div>吾心动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213181_comment'></div>汝侍几筵，吾今趋泸南省尊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213181_comment'></div>予未有以应，兄奋曰：「吾决矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213181_comment'></div>是夕裹粮，黎明走洪川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213181_comment'></div>将僦舟，而江水盛怒，声摇数十里，客舟布岸，皆相顾不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213181_comment'></div>兄彷徨堤上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213181_comment'></div>有渔者持小艇系港中，啖以厚利，不诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213181_comment'></div>兄跳入，据艇中，叱仆夫解维，渔者不得已从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213181_comment'></div>用二日半至泸，而先公果病甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213181_comment'></div>见兄大惊，诘其所以来，兄具道曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213181_comment'></div>先公叹曰：「天告汝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213181_comment'></div>是日疾少间，兄具大舟迎侍以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213181_comment'></div>居数日，疾复作，遂卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213181_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213181_comment'></div>方是之时，非兄孝足以通神，诚足以知几，其祸可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213181_comment'></div>元符二年冬，弟庾以贡举事系狱临邛，语连兄，临邛并械之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213181_comment'></div>凡对吏逾年，掠治无完肤，而其词确然不及庾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213181_comment'></div>以故狱久不具，卒会赦，除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213181_comment'></div>其坚忍如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213181_comment'></div>兄性真率无威仪，人多易之，至是乃大服，以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1213181_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1213181_comment'></div>吾少兄十有五年，年二十五即去为吏四方，五年十年乃一归，归不过旬月复去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1213181_comment'></div>此其中宁能无轶事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1213181_comment'></div>然其大节可睹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1213181_comment'></div>兄以崇宁五年五月二十一日卒于家，而贫不即葬，殡僧舍十有三年，然后得归骨于某村之原，时政和八年十一月日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1213181_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1213181'>兄讳瞻，改伯虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1213181_comment'></div>始字望之，今长孺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1213181_comment'></div>氏于唐，望于鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1213181_comment'></div>五十二年，卒归土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1213181_comment'></div>夫人范，前物故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1213181_comment'></div>葬用周制，以范祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1213181_comment'></div>男子二，才一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1213181_comment'></div>男业儒释，女犹处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1213181_comment'></div>墓用铭，家有谱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1213181_comment'></div>后世参之，考其素。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1213181_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年十一月一日</a>　为姨母作墓铭。作品：《史夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1213187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213187?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和八年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213187")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213187_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213187'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213187'>夹江县孙公讳某之夫人姓史氏，眉州青神人，故任嘉州军事推官讳著明之曾孙，故赠大理寺丞讳昭吉之孙，余外祖讳及之季女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213187_comment'></div>余少时尝至其家矣，公长不逾中人，语音如钟，喜谈前言往行，亹亹可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213187_comment'></div>盖尝约家事勿复相关，悉听夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213187_comment'></div>夫人明敏解事，通人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213187_comment'></div>其规模措置，有绝人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213187_comment'></div>孙氏岁入不赀，用度亦广矣，而夫人治之皆有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213187_comment'></div>内外亲戚姻娅之间，冠昏宾祭庆吊之事，殆无虚日，而夫人处之，皆有体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213187_comment'></div>公三娶，男女九人，而夫人待之皆如己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213187_comment'></div>余尝阴察之，未尝见其有毫发轻重厚薄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213187_comment'></div>方是时，长子昌龄，年四十馀，喜从余游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213187_comment'></div>幼子昌裔，年十五六，昼出从师受书，夜归，夫人自教之，至夜分乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213187_comment'></div>女有适罗某者，有适王某者，有适魏某而蚤卒者，有适张某者，有适宋某者，有未笄者，有绝幼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213187_comment'></div>是岁绍圣元年甲戌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213187_comment'></div>今二十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213187_comment'></div>公先卒，既葬，夫人又卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213187_comment'></div>今葬矣，昌龄亦卒，孙七人，曾孙三人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213187_comment'></div>昌裔今名衍，孙七人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213187_comment'></div>向之未笄者，今嫁承议郎鲜于某，有封号矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213187_comment'></div>向之绝幼者，今为某人妻，有子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213187_comment'></div>人欲无老，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213187_comment'></div>夫人貌类先妣孺人，卒然遇之，几不能辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213187_comment'></div>先妣既没，余以画者失真，恐无以示后，因取夫人传神临之，见者无不陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213187_comment'></div>其兄弟之间盖如此，然则铭其墓者，非余而谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213187_comment'></div>夫人享年七十一，其卒也，以政和四年十一月五日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213187_comment'></div>其葬也，以八年十一月一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213187_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1213187'>丰泉之原，封若斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213187_comment'></div>祔而合之，盖从鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213187_comment'></div>其甥铭之，固其所。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1213187_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　集“三谢诗”，并作文附于诗后。作品：《书<三谢诗>后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称是年唐庚赴京师，与黄鹏异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书三谢诗后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213125")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213125'>江左诸谢，诗文见《文选》者六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213125_comment'></div>希逸无诗，宣远、叔源有诗，不工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213125_comment'></div>今取灵运、惠连、玄晖诗，合六十四篇，为《三谢诗》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213125_comment'></div>是三人者，诗至玄晖语益工，然萧散自得之趣，亦复少减，渐有唐风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213125_comment'></div>于此可以观世变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213125_comment'></div>唐子西书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1213125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年冬</a>　与强幼安遇于城东景德僧舍，论诗谈文，作诗记之。作品：《次韵强幼安冬日旅舍》<span class='inlineComment2'>（强幼安二十年后整理追记，得《文录》一卷，凡三十五条。）</span><div id='poem_520284' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520284' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520284?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵强幼安冬日旅舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520284")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520284_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520284'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520284'>残岁无多日，此身犹旅人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520284'>客情安枕少，天气举杯频。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520284'>桂玉黄金尽，风埃白发新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520284'>异乡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_520284", 520284, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>梅信</span>远，谁寄一枝春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520284_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520284'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520284_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年十二月一日</a>　在京师，有文记《寅申录》文集。作品：《书姑苏张自强教谕编<寅申录>》<div id='poem_1213124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书姑苏张自强教授所编寅申录</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213124")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213124'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213124'>吾平生取名以此，其掇谤亦以此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213124_comment'></div>顷谪惠州，过扶胥，此书失手坠海中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213124_comment'></div>舟人皆失色，予独喜，幸名与谤都息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213124_comment'></div>不为今日复稍见于士大夫间，读之惘然，似他人文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213124_comment'></div>思之茫然，如隔世事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213124_comment'></div>而姑苏张自强复持此六卷示予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213124_comment'></div>是名与谤特未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213124_comment'></div>然自强嗜吾文，必知我者也，必爱我者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213124_comment'></div>想能为我深藏而慎出之，庶几可以免夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213124_comment'></div>宣和己亥十二月一日，眉山唐子西书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1213124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: 成都

<div class='label1' id='f05152064efd49d18f552fb7f1928429_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f05152064efd49d18f552fb7f1928429");'><span id='f05152064efd49d18f552fb7f1928429_link'
