href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　华阳尉任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年正月十四日</a>　华阳尉任上，有文。作品：《慰国恤表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在太学，于八、九月谒东坡于京师，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称《慰国恤表》当作于唐庚31岁时，是年皇太后卒，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慰国恤表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年正月十四日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213075")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213075'>伏准遗诰，皇太后以正月十四日上升者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213075_comment'></div>发开驿讣，宣示郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213075_comment'></div>狂号失声，震悼丧魄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中慰。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213075_comment'></div>恭惟大行皇太后家顺以巽，坤柔而刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213075_comment'></div>决大策于禁中，指麾而定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213075_comment'></div>成治功于天下，退托不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213075_comment'></div>有姜任妇德之贤，非汉唐母后之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213075_comment'></div>向婴疾疢，本自忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213075_comment'></div>瞑眩弗瘳，弥留遽及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213075_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下深仁赋性，纯孝因心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213075_comment'></div>方攀慕于宝慈，谅何堪于荼毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213075_comment'></div>然以宗祧任重，军国事丛，愿宽罔极之哀，少副有生之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213075_comment'></div>臣忝郡寄，不获奔诣阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213075_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1213075_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　华阳尉任上，有文上入蜀使者。作品：《上宪使书》<div id='poem_1213086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宪使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1093年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213086")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213086'>某窃惟阁下奉使入蜀，首尾三年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213086_comment'></div>蜀中搢绅士大夫与夫四方之游宦于蜀者，不知其几何人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213086_comment'></div>扬眉吐气求出于门下者，亦不知其几何人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213086_comment'></div>求而得者几何人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213086_comment'></div>求而不得者几何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213086_comment'></div>应者有尽而求者无穷，意者阁下亦厌而鄙之否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213086_comment'></div>某尝思之，此非独士人之罪，时使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213086_comment'></div>先王之世，所以进退天下人材之术，与今大异，盖自尧舜时已有三载考绩、三考黜陟幽明之说，至于成周而其法大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213086_comment'></div>官府群吏，日考其成，月考其要，岁终则冢宰考其会而议废置，三岁则王者大计而诛赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213086_comment'></div>当是之时，才者有所劝，不才者无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213086_comment'></div>凡所以正其位，进其治，作其事，制其食者，莫不有先后之叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213086_comment'></div>故士皆安分乐业，惟上之所进退，曷尝有此奔竞驰骛之风哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213086_comment'></div>周道衰，先王之法坏，凡上之所以进退天下之士者，一切出于保任荐举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213086_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213086_comment'></div>保任荐举之法行，则奔竞驰骛之风作，此理之自然，势之必致也，岂独士人之罪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213086_comment'></div>孟子曰：「士之仕也，犹农夫之耕也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213086_comment'></div>其失位也，犹诸侯之失国家也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213086_comment'></div>无田则不祭，出疆则载质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213086_comment'></div>士之进取，固不足多责，独论其正与不正尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213086_comment'></div>某迂昧寡合，众所非笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213086_comment'></div>独阁下恻然以为可教，奖借诲谕，似非偶然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213086_comment'></div>方此依赖，而遽闻阁下有使吴之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213086_comment'></div>虽欲长侍下风，可复得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213086_comment'></div>是用忘其鄙陋，而妄有说于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213086_comment'></div>伏惟阁下观先王所以进退人材与近世不同，怜士之进取，实系于时而宽假之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213086_comment'></div>不胜幸愿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1213086_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　华阳任满，赴益昌判司任治狱事，有诗。作品：《赴益昌二首》<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520312'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520312'>元气脱形数，运动<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作回）</span>天地内。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520312'>东坡未离人，岂比元气大。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520312'>天地不能容，伸舒辄有碍。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520312'>低头不能仰，闭口焉敢欬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520312'>东坡坦率老，局促因<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作应）</span>难耐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520312'>何当与道俱，逍遥天地外。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520312_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520312'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_520312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　益昌判司任，有文。作品：《上钱宪杂文序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在利州治狱掾，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上钱宪杂文序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213126")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213126'>宪使钱公按益昌，命某献其所为文，意将有以教之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213126_comment'></div>承命欣跃，退求平生所业，而多难沦失，存者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213126_comment'></div>其间复有俳谐者，放荡者，触时忌者，不近道者，妄论天下利害非所当言者，文多不足录者，为故纸糊窗、首尾讹缺莫可考者，率皆削去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213126_comment'></div>得古赋一首，《汉漂母碑》一首，《竹轩记》一首，古乐府二首，近体诗一十九首，并序为二十五首以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213126_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213126_comment'></div>士之自鬻，非古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213126_comment'></div>惟某不能自鬻，以取困于时，然亦以此得出于门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213126_comment'></div>而公亦信其决非自鬻者，庶几可以受教而无嫌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213126_comment'></div>谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1213126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　益昌判司任，有诗塑造讲道义、轻钱财、傲权贵的平民形象。作品：《张求》<div id='poem_193146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张求</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_193146")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193146'>张求一老兵，著帽如破斗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193146'>卖卜益昌市，性命寄杯酒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193146'>骑马好事人，金钱投瓮牖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193146'>一语不假借，意自有臧否。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193146'>鸡肋巧安拳，未省怕嗔殴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193146'>坐此益寒酸，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_193146", 193146, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>饿理</span>将入口。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193146'>未死且强项，那暇顾炙手。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193146'>士节久凋丧，舐痔甜不呕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193146'>求岂知道者，议论无所苟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193146'>吾宁<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作欲）</span>从之游，聊以激衰朽。<div id='poem_sentence_9_193146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_193146'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_193146_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　益昌判司任，有诗谴责庸吏。作品：《讯囚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称《讯囚》作于其27岁时，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_193145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_193145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/193145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>讯囚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1095年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_193145")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_193145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_193145'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_193145'>参军坐厅事，据案嚼齿牙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_193145'>引囚到庭下，囚口争喧哗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_193145'>参军气益振，声厉语更忉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_193145'>“自古官中财，一一民膏血。<div id='poem_sentence_3_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_193145'>为吏掌管钥，反窃以自私。<div id='poem_sentence_4_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_193145'>人不汝谁何，如摘颔下髭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_193145'>事老<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作久）</span>恶自彰，证佐日月明。<div id='poem_sentence_6_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_193145'>推穷见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_193145", 193145, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>毛脉</span>，那可口舌争”。<div id='poem_sentence_7_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_193145'>有囚奋然出，请与参军辨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_193145'>“参军心如眼，有睫不自见。<div id='poem_sentence_9_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_193145'>参军在场屋，薄薄有声称。<div id='poem_sentence_10_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_193145'>只今作参军，几时得骞腾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_193145'>无功食国禄，去窃能几何。<div id='poem_sentence_12_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_193145'>上官乃容隐，曾不加谴诃。<div id='poem_sentence_13_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_193145'>囚今信有罪，参军宜揣分。<div id='poem_sentence_14_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_193145'>等是为贫计，何苦独相困”。<div id='poem_sentence_15_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_193145'>参军噤无语，反顾吏卒嗟<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作羞）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_193145'>包裹琴与书，明日吾归休。<div id='poem_sentence_17_193145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_193145'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_193145_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　任益昌参军，时邻西郡县边事紧急，多涉军事，忙碌不堪，有诗。作品：《自笑二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在利州治狱掾，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称《自笑二首》作于其27岁时，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_520433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520433' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自笑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520433")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520433'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520433'>已白穷经首，仍丹许国心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520433_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520433'>那能天补绽，更欲海填深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520433_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520433'>儿馁嗔郎罢，妻寒望<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作怨）</span>藁砧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520433_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520433'>世间南北路，何用尔沾襟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520433_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520433'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520433_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　益昌参军任上，王观复离任，有赠序。作品：《送王观复序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称《送王观复序》当作于唐庚30岁时，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王观复序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213121")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213121'>绍圣丙子岁，予官益昌，始从吾友王观复游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213121_comment'></div>方是时，其文已如击石拊石，诚非世俗之乐，独音节未和尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213121_comment'></div>其后四年，相会于南隆，复得其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213121_comment'></div>读之遂觉雍容调畅，取意论事，益有条绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213121_comment'></div>庶几乎八音克谐，无相夺伦者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213121_comment'></div>予方耸然异之，求其说而未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213121_comment'></div>或者便谓涪翁在黔中，观复以诗书相切磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213121_comment'></div>涪翁奇之，相与反复论难，因书柳子厚效渊明古体诗十数解示之，俾知昔人文章低昂疏密之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213121_comment'></div>疑其有得于此，是未必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213121_comment'></div>然吾视观复比来日益就道，盖更事愈多，见善愈明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213121_comment'></div>少年锐气扫灭殆尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213121_comment'></div>收歛反约，渐有归宿，宜其见于文字者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213121_comment'></div>吾何以知其然也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213121_comment'></div>人之精神何与于琴，而几动于心则声应于指，自然冥合，有不可诘者，而况于文乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213121_comment'></div>文主于气，气熟而文和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213121_comment'></div>此理之决然，无足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213121_comment'></div>盖涪翁所告者法也，余所论者理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213121_comment'></div>告之以法，而观复又日进于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213121_comment'></div>今其归也，自言从苏子于湘南，过涪翁于宜城，又将尽得其所谓法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213121_comment'></div>则观复之于文，岂特如是而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213121_comment'></div>观复其勉之哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1213121_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1097')">1096-1097年</a>　益昌参军任上，有文。作品：《箕踞轩记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（据清抄本所署，此文作于绍圣三年五月二十日，作者时为益昌判司。其文表面藐视礼法，实则不满于判司官至卑微，而自视屈才。）</span>《贺杨运判启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在利州治狱掾，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span>《上监司书》<div id='poem_1213164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>箕踞轩记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍圣三年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1096年五月二十日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213164")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213164'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213164'>箕踞者，山间之容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213164_comment'></div>拳腰耸肩，抱膝而危坐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213164_comment'></div>伛偻跼缩，其圆如箕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213164_comment'></div>故古人谓之箕踞，便于赋诗，便于阅书，便于长啸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213164_comment'></div>其势如蹲猿，如投竿而渔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213164_comment'></div>盖长松之下，滩石之上，放然不拘礼法者之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213164_comment'></div>以之事上则不恭，以之临下则不庄，以之待贤者则有所不可，以之遇众人，则有所不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213164_comment'></div>故古之士大夫矜名检饰边幅者，皆鄙而不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213164_comment'></div>予今以五斗红腐置身于忧患之场，是非利害汹汹百出，以一身之微，受无穷之责，目视上带，则辄取怪怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213164_comment'></div>方且远谗畏讥，规规然从事于礼法，柔声和容，敛版罄折，拜揖跪起，以取媚于世，惟恐其不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213164_comment'></div>而以「箕踞」名轩，岂不异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213164_comment'></div>盖官舍之西，旧有轩数间，直堂屋之后，人事之所不及，宾客游从之所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213164_comment'></div>往往独游于此，解衣盘薄，箕踞于胡床之上，含爪赋诗，曝背阅书，以释其忽忽不平之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213164_comment'></div>临风长啸，而草木为之萧然，足以见其诞率如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213164_comment'></div>而犹有所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213164_comment'></div>虽有所畏，而诞率之性，终不能少贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213164_comment'></div>亦施之处己，而不以接物，则庶几其无患也，故以「箕踞」名之，而为文以见其所以名之之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213164_comment'></div>绍圣三年五月二十日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1213164_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1213099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺杨运判启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213099")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213099'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213099'>伏审宠膺宸命，荣抱使权，爰择刚辰，已谐礼上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213099_comment'></div>凡叨属部，举切欣悰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213099_comment'></div>某累任剑东，粗知民俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213099_comment'></div>虽人贫地瘠，顾岁入之不饶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213099_comment'></div>而吏禄军储，亦年计之足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213099_comment'></div>傥货源之不遏，宜利孔之并兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213099_comment'></div>驯致羡馀，式资经画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213099_comment'></div>恭惟某官才猷强济，术略疏通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213099_comment'></div>入握省兰，已振望郎之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213099_comment'></div>出持漕节，用昭烦使之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213099_comment'></div>谅生财之有方，不加赋而自给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213099_comment'></div>伫腾最目，行陟华途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213099_comment'></div>某方隶旄麾，敢论瓜葛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213099_comment'></div>雅故未忘于一日，庇庥当赖于二天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213099_comment'></div>欢抃所丛，端倪曷喻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1213099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年正月甲寅</a>　代作贺表。作品：《贺进筑表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在利州治狱掾，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称《贺进筑表》作于其29岁时，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
剑阁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f765d0d0cf4b4cf7a9476a738d856166_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f765d0d0cf4b4cf7a9476a738d856166");'><span id='f765d0d0cf4b4cf7a9476a738d856166_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>，28岁</div><div id='f765d0d0cf4b4cf7a9476a738d856166' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　益昌任满，赴绵州主管学事，于剑州道中作诗。作品：《剑州道中见桃李盛开，而梅花犹有存者》<div id='poem_520359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>剑州道中见桃李盛开而梅花犹有存者<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本下有漫赋短歌四字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520359")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520359'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520359'>桃花能红李能白，春深无<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作何）</span>处无颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520359'>不应尚有数枝梅，可是东君苦留客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520359'>向来开处当严冬，桃李未在交游中<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作白者红未红）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520359'>即今已是丈人行，勿<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作肯）</span>与年少争春风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520359'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520359_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绵阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b5df2c94b96544a5abe1f9b189d4d1e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b5df2c94b96544a5abe1f9b189d4d1e9");'><span id='b5df2c94b96544a5abe1f9b189d4d1e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1099')">1098-1099年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='b5df2c94b96544a5abe1f9b189d4d1e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在绵州主管学事，为安惇作贺启。作品：《贺安谏议启》<div id='poem_1213097' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213097' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213097?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺安谏议启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1098年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213097")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213097_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213097'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213097'>伏审光奉制纶，擢居谏苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213097_comment'></div>朝廷增重，中外耸闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213097_comment'></div>窃以致君泽民，圣贤之所易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213097_comment'></div>逢时遇主，古今之至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213097_comment'></div>当谏行言听之时，居面折庭争之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213097_comment'></div>得伸其志，实系于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213097_comment'></div>共惟某官酝藉深醇，议论辩博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213097_comment'></div>养慷慨敢言之气，负纵横适用之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213097_comment'></div>必将论列是非，敷陈利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213097_comment'></div>然恐供职未几，别有九迁之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213097_comment'></div>遇事辄言，安俟七年之久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213097_comment'></div>某荷知有素，称庆无缘，欣抃之私，实倍夷等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1213097_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在绵州主管学事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阆中
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ef29723cb2ca46f18e3661581ed17193_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ef29723cb2ca46f18e3661581ed17193");'><span id='ef29723cb2ca46f18e3661581ed17193_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1104')">1100-1104年</a>，30-34岁</div><div id='ef29723cb2ca46f18e3661581ed17193' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　绵州受代有日，旋任阆中令，为苏俞书斋作记。作品：《愚斋记》<div id='poem_1213162' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213162' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213162?labeling=true' target='_blank'>愚斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213162")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213162_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213162'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213162'>元符三年，洛阳苏公通守南隆，治书室于厅事之东偏，名之曰「愚斋」，而属某为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213162_comment'></div>某言于公曰：愚有等级，公将安处也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213162_comment'></div>有颜子之愚，有高柴之愚，有宁武子之愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213162_comment'></div>扬子以晁错为愚，柳子厚自以为愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213162_comment'></div>颜子之愚，《老子》所谓盛德者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213162_comment'></div>高柴之愚，《中庸》所谓不及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213162_comment'></div>宁武子之愚，则《诗》所谓「亦维斯戾」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213162_comment'></div>晁错之愚，则《语》所谓古之直者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213162_comment'></div>若夫柳子厚之愚，则事载方册，有不可诬者，文章学术为当代所宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213162_comment'></div>自唐以来，论当世大儒，则必称韩、柳，而自以为愚，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213162_comment'></div>然贞元之党，妇人女子皆知其必败，而柳子独不悟也，谓之不愚，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213162_comment'></div>是数子者，其愚固有等级，公将安处也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213162_comment'></div>以为高柴之愚，则才非不及于道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213162_comment'></div>以为宁武子之愚，则生非不逢于时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213162_comment'></div>以为晁错之愚，则无吴、楚之变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213162_comment'></div>以为柳子厚之愚，则无伾、文之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213162_comment'></div>某将处公以颜子之愚，则公岂有意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213162_comment'></div>公平生聚书万卷，手不停披，既以自得于心矣，推其绪馀以教诸子，皆卓然有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213162_comment'></div>其长子大寿以文学知名于时，而公犹以愚自处，此真有意于所谓盛德者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213162_comment'></div>《传》曰：「晞颜之人，亦颜之徒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213162_comment'></div>公何辞焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213162_comment'></div>请以是为记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213162_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1213162'>伾：原阙，据四部丛刊本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1213162_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1213162'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1213162_0'>⑴ 《唐先生文集》卷一五。又见《圣宋文选》卷二三，《古今合璧事类备要》续集卷三七，《古今事文类聚》别集卷一九，《八代文钞》第三八册，同治《南部县志》卷二八。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1213162_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　为通判苏俞书斋作诗二首。作品：《苏君俞通判愚斋二首》<div id='poem_520398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏君俞通判愚斋二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520398")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_520398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520398'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520398'>人间争以智相高，底事纷纷祗自劳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520398'>顿觉朱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>愚真有味，莫将佳处语儿曹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520398'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_520398_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_520398'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_520398_0'>⑴ 任本作宋，汪本作味</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_520398_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_520399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520399?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_520399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520399'>三年消遣琴书在，一室清虚杖履凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520399'>却怪斋名浑未尽，迩来愚智已兼忘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_520399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏俞唱和，公再作诗答之。作品：《通判苏君俞见和，复次韵答之》<div id='poem_520335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通判苏君俞见和复次韵答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520335")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520335'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520335'>公才过人其<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作真）</span>倍十<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作真十倍）</span>，词艺即今谁跂及。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520335'>万卷收藏富编集，诗人阃域称优入。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520335'>西州书生学穿执，朅<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作迩）</span>来东游为丝<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作禄）</span>粒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520335'>十分折腰敢长揖，欲吐壮怀还自吸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520335'>朋从调笑斗捷给，狂言偶发难收拾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520335'>语意俳谐韵牵絷，不敢献公公密缉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520335'>报章大是鲛人泣，一一珠玑落圆湿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_520335'>自惭思竭如空笈，口吻悲吟知<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作殊）</span>窘急。<div id='poem_sentence_7_520335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_520335'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_520335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　有文。作品：《颜鲁公祠堂记》<div id='poem_1213165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213165?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颜鲁公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213165")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213165'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213165'>上元中，颜鲁公为蓬州长史，过新政，作《离堆记》四百馀言，书而刻之石壁上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213165_comment'></div>字径三寸，虽崩坏剥裂之馀，而典刑具在，使人见之，凛然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213165_comment'></div>元符三年，余友马强叔来尹是邑，始为公作祠堂于其侧，而求文以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213165_comment'></div>余谓仁之胜不仁久矣，然有时乎不胜，而反为所陷焉者，命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213165_comment'></div>史臣论公晚节偃蹇，为奸臣所挤，见陨贼手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213165_comment'></div>是未必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213165_comment'></div>公孙丞相以仲舒相胶西，梁冀以张纲守广陵，李逢吉以韩愈使镇州，而庐杞以公使希烈，其用意正相类尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213165_comment'></div>然于数君子者，终不能有所伤，而公独不免于虎口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213165_comment'></div>由是观之，士之成败存亡，岂不有命耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213165_comment'></div>而小人轩然自以为得计，不亦谬乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213165_comment'></div>且吾闻古之尚友者，以友天下之善士为未足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213165_comment'></div>又尚论古之人，诵其诗，读其书，思见其人而不可得，则方且欲招屈子于江滨，起士会于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213165_comment'></div>盖其志之所愿，则超然相慕于数千百载之外，而况于公乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213165_comment'></div>公之功名事业既已绝人，而文字之妙亦不可及，因其心画之所在而祠之，此亦昔人尚友之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213165_comment'></div>尝试与强叔登离堆，探石堂，观其遗迹，而味其平生，则公之精神风采，犹或可以想见也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213165_comment'></div>年月日记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1213165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1213165_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年四月</a>　韩忠彦为右仆射，代人作贺启。作品：《贺右仆射韩相公启》<div id='poem_1213094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺右仆射韩相公启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213094")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213094'>伏审显奉制麻，延登宰席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213094_comment'></div>播腾九有，欢庆一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213094_comment'></div>窃闻考元龟以断大谋，不如旧德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213094_comment'></div>指乔木而称故国，未若世臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213094_comment'></div>才猷夙著于庙堂，名实已隆于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213094_comment'></div>故社稷因之而倚重，而朝廷恃此以稽疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213094_comment'></div>恭惟某官器重海涵，神清玉粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213094_comment'></div>天资攸禀，有仁民爱物之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213094_comment'></div>家学所传，皆论道经邦之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213094_comment'></div>蔼扬令闻，坦涉亨途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213094_comment'></div>顷任枢躔，谋已深于汉幄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213094_comment'></div>出临阃寄，泽未溥于商霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213094_comment'></div>政地久虚，佥言允属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213094_comment'></div>值圣朝之嗣服，思辅相以迓衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213094_comment'></div>召还三迁，遂宅百揆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213094_comment'></div>韦、平盛事，固无愧于古人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213094_comment'></div>房、杜全功，诚责成于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213094_comment'></div>必将尽发胸中之蕴，庶几大慰海内之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213094_comment'></div>某承乏遐陬，侧闻除目，阻远潭潭之府，莫趋两两之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213094_comment'></div>丛抃寸诚，难形尺牍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1213094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　代作贺启。作品：《贺门下李侍郎启》<div id='poem_1213095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213095?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺门下李侍郎启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213095")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213095_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213095'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213095'>伏审拜恩中陛，秉政东台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213095_comment'></div>凡与生成，举深欣怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213095_comment'></div>窃以明良之会，今昔所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213095_comment'></div>董、贾有志，而竟不逢时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213095_comment'></div>房、杜得君，而未能及礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213095_comment'></div>故汉功不过于如此，而唐政亦终于阒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213095_comment'></div>追还古初，意在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213095_comment'></div>恭惟某官识探道奥，学济圣涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213095_comment'></div>经天纬地之文，得之性禀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213095_comment'></div>尊主庇民之略，尽在术中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213095_comment'></div>早跻华途，夙著时望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213095_comment'></div>西垣润色，灿追典诰之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213095_comment'></div>右辖论思，肃振维纲之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213095_comment'></div>顷从凤阁，出守麟符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213095_comment'></div>众人叹其失时，君子知其复用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213095_comment'></div>值圣神之嗣服，思耆旧以迓衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213095_comment'></div>召还自外而任以春官，曾未阅时而入居左省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213095_comment'></div>除音所彻，众议允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213095_comment'></div>必将尽摅胸臆之奇，庶几大慰迩遐之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213095_comment'></div>某久依琳馆，尝辱钧陶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213095_comment'></div>激欢抃于重衿，难叙陈于弱翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213095_comment'></div>伫闻爰立，益副具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213095_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1213095_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年四月</a>　代程守作贺表。作品：《贺天宁节表》<div id='poem_1213068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺天宁节表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代程守）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213068'>穹昊储休，将永熙明之祚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213068_comment'></div>圣神应运，丕承大定之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213068_comment'></div>鸣社在晨，际天共庆<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213068_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下寅恭克己，孚惠得心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213068_comment'></div>自然尧舜之仁，故能济众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213068_comment'></div>醇用成康之化，几致措刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213068_comment'></div>政已逮于中和，国遂臻于康靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213068_comment'></div>爰纪诞弥之节，宜增逸乐之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213068_comment'></div>目断觚棱，莫缀称觞之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213068_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1213068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年七月</a>　在阆州任上，有贺启。作品：《贺蒋枢密启》<div id='poem_1213096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺蒋枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213096")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213096'>伏审诞敷明命，擢贰鸿枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213096_comment'></div>世稔服于重名，人共欣于显拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213096_comment'></div>恭惟某官才高康济，志切经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213096_comment'></div>文章秀发于妙龄，器业养成于晚节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213096_comment'></div>中外荐更之久，所守益完；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213096_comment'></div>纵横应变之材，无施不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213096_comment'></div>出而颇、牧，入则卿、云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213096_comment'></div>先帝深知，欲大用而未果；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213096_comment'></div>嗣皇优眷，遂图任而无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213096_comment'></div>召还自外，而归直禁林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213096_comment'></div>曾未阅时，而延登右府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213096_comment'></div>参裁机政，宁穆邦猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213096_comment'></div>朝廷取决于坐筹，边鄙折冲于燕俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213096_comment'></div>君臣千载，孰窥造膝之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213096_comment'></div>冠带百蛮，行见止戈之武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213096_comment'></div>某侧闻除目，阻远钧严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213096_comment'></div>莫伸贺厦之私，永愧登门之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213096_comment'></div>其如欢跃，罔喻端倪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213096_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1213096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_520369'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520369'>岁华忽忽又清明，忆与诸生试集英。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520369_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在阆州任上，有文寄情山水草木。作品：《有翠亭铭》<div id='poem_1213173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213173?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有翠亭铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213173")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1213173_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213173'>山不远人，人自远山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1213173'>见即为易，有之为难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1213173'>陇上牧儿，林间樵叟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1213173'>虽能得之，而不可有。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1213173'>贵戚买园，宠侯赐宅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1213173'>虽或有之，而不可得。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1213173'>惟吾放浪，与是有缘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1213173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　在阆州任上，作文以梅自况，抒生不逢时之感慨。作品：《惜梅赋》<div id='poem_1213061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惜梅赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213061")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213061'>阆中县庭有梅，株甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213061_comment'></div>正当庭中，出入者患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213061_comment'></div>有劝予以伐去者，为作《惜梅赋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213061_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1213061'>县庭有梅株焉，吾不知植于何时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213061_comment'></div>荫一亩其疏疏，香数里其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1213061", 1213061, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>披披</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213061_comment'></div>侵小雪而更繁，得胧月而益奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213061_comment'></div>然生不得其地，俗物溷其幽姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213061_comment'></div>前胥史之纷拿，后囚系之嘤咿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213061_comment'></div>虽物性之自适，揆人意而非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213061_comment'></div>既不得荐嘉实于商鼎，效微劳于魏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213061_comment'></div>又不得托孤根于竹间，遂野性于水涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213061_comment'></div>怅驿使之未逢，惊羌笛之频吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213061_comment'></div>恐飘零之易及，虽清绝而安施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213061_comment'></div>客犹以为妨贤也，而讽予以伐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213061_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213061_comment'></div>吾闻幽兰之美瑞，乃以当户而见夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213061_comment'></div>兹昔人之所短，顾仁者之所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213061_comment'></div>吾宁迂数步之行，而假以一席之地，对寒艳而把酒，嗅清香而赋诗可也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1213061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　六月，始修阆中敕书楼，唐庚亲董其役，十二月成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年正月十五日</a>　在阆州任上，为新修敕书楼作记。作品：《新修敕书楼记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年七月离阆中，赴官绵州（今四川绵阳）任录事参军，到任后游览绵州名胜，作《登越王楼》《将家游治平院盖老杜所谓东津也》《游天池院》等诗，并于是年十月八日，与弟庾重登越王楼，作《十月十八日与舍弟同登越王楼便道趋开元寺上天池得句满纸颠倒杂乱几不可读明日诠次成二十二韵》诗，与黄鹏所记异，黄鹏并未提及绵州任事，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213166?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新修敕书楼记<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁二年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年正月十五日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213166")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213166_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213166'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213166'>始余未至阆中，闻其为剧邑也，意其官府制度，诸事有体，称古子男之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213166_comment'></div>既至，入门见其所谓「敕书楼」者，庳屋数楹，椽腐瓦疏，将过其下者，则必却盖俛首，鞭马疾趋，凛然惟恐其欲压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213166_comment'></div>顾而疑之，以为县治于此，不知几何年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213166_comment'></div>令之从者，亦不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213166_comment'></div>楼在厅事之前，非思虑之所不及，然皆更相因仍无改作者，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213166_comment'></div>既而究之，乃不足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213166_comment'></div>始，宣德郎孙君袭既新厅堂，尝议及矣，未果作而受代去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213166_comment'></div>奉议郎李君观继修库狱，复有意于是矣，以饥而寝其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213166_comment'></div>至余号为愚蠢无知，锐然直前，而不顾利害者也，然犹尺寸积累，二年而后有作，亲董其役，数月而后有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213166_comment'></div>盖自二君以迄于今，更阅三闰，然后得以一变其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213166_comment'></div>呜呼，何其难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213166_comment'></div>而况兴利除害，立事建功，规为措置，有大于此者，不又难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213166_comment'></div>以余成之之难，有以知二君欲为之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213166_comment'></div>以二君欲为之难，有以知前人更相因仍，历年滋久而无所改作者，彼非安于如此也，盖势不足以使人，力不足以行意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213166_comment'></div>举手动作，左窒右碍，终日忧畏，而不得以遂其所欲为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213166_comment'></div>此人之为吏所以无功，天下之事所以不立，而有志者所以永叹也，何独此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213166_comment'></div>何足怪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213166_comment'></div>楼屋上下十间，馀材为吏舍十有七间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213166_comment'></div>始于元年之六月，成于十二月，而余去以二年之七月云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213166_comment'></div>崇宁二年正月十五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1213166_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年二月</a>　作文思生母史夫人。作品：《史夫人行状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年在绵州任录事参军，春作《上俞漕书》，初夏游仙云宫，作《修仙云宫》诗，初秋作《率诸人饮开元寺勉翁有诗因次其韵》诗，冬作《游雪峰院书所见院在开元寺之西越王楼之东盖小院也》诗等，与黄鹏所记异，黄鹏并未提及绵州任事，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史夫人行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213179")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213179'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213179'>夫人史氏，眉州青神县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213179_comment'></div>嘉州军事推官讳著明之曾孙，大理寺丞讳昭吉之孙，进士讳及之女，鲁国先生讳某之配也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213179_comment'></div>先生喜宾客，重然诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213179_comment'></div>视金钱如泥，无分毫顾惜，不论多寡，费尽乃已，竟坐此贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213179_comment'></div>而夫人处之怡然自得，其为善之乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213179_comment'></div>先生自言：「吾六岁而孤，勤苦自立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213179_comment'></div>取名于时，岂有兄弟教哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213179_comment'></div>常持是说，未尝督责三子以学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213179_comment'></div>而夫人则不然，躬课诸郎读书，至丙夜乃寝，率以是为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213179_comment'></div>平生无所好，独闻诵书声辄欣然，盖性之所嗜如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213179_comment'></div>夫人不逮事舅姑，事先生如事父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213179_comment'></div>治饮食以进，必立侍，须彻馔乃去，或者以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213179_comment'></div>元祐三年春，先生遇疾几殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213179_comment'></div>夫人焚香祷祈，愿以身代死，家人止之，不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213179_comment'></div>俄而疾暴作，掷香炉于地，扶掖就枕，已不知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213179_comment'></div>后六日夫人病笃，而先生疾稍间，先生竟愈，而夫人遂不起，时二月二十日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213179_comment'></div>初，夫人之祈死也，先生疾革不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213179_comment'></div>夫人既卒，诸子以事告，先生哀甚，为诗以哭之，闻者莫不泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213179_comment'></div>夫人享年五十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213179_comment'></div>某，其子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213179_comment'></div>某，其婿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213179_comment'></div>某，其孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213179_comment'></div>孙女二人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213179_comment'></div>崇宁三年二月二十八日，从先生葬于丹棱县鼓面山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213179_comment'></div>先生道虽不行于民，其行于家者盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213179_comment'></div>非先生何以当夫人之贤，观夫人足以知先生之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213179_comment'></div>此其子庚所以必欲状其行以传于人，予所以不得而辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213179_comment'></div>呜呼，诚亦可书也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213179_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1213179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　作文思长者程公仪。作品：《祭程公仪文》<div id='poem_1213192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭程公仪文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213192")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213192'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213192'>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213192_comment'></div>我昔携孥，赴官益昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213192_comment'></div>公时送我，泣下沾裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213192_comment'></div>云我老矣，不复见子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213192_comment'></div>终天之别，将止于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213192_comment'></div>我谓不然，愿翁加飧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213192_comment'></div>秩满即还，弹指顷间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213192_comment'></div>我舟既行，翁止于岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213192_comment'></div>眷眷不去，回首永叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213192_comment'></div>我官于东，转眼十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213192_comment'></div>复来寻翁，墓木苍烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213192_comment'></div>永怀往事，泪落秋草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213192_comment'></div>为文写哀，以荐蘋藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213192_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1213192_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　阆州任满，以常调凤州教授，作诗自宽。作品：《除凤州教授，非所愿也，作此自宽》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚除凤州教授在崇宁四年，与黄鹏所记异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_520343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除凤州教授非所欲也作此自宽</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520343")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520343'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520343'>人生才食顷，何处分好弱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520343'>刑狱即道场，筦库有真乐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520343'>故纸终日翻，毛锥几年阁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520343'>百函无力致，诸公谁说著。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520343'>今承学校乏，颇讶名字错。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520343'>宿业岂无恋，得冶不敢跃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520343'>骨肉远难俱，囊装贫易缚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_520343'>师儒要好手，老大良非脚。<div id='poem_sentence_7_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_520343'>戛尽识羹空，抽穷知茧薄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_520343'>后生端所<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本作可）</span>畏，人材若<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作君）</span>为作。<div id='poem_sentence_9_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_520343'>岂唯嘲孝先，更恐困有若。<div id='poem_sentence_10_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_520343'>行路固知难，得地幸不恶。<div id='poem_sentence_11_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_520343'>柳拖千丈丝，山集五色雀。<div id='poem_sentence_12_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_520343'>绛纱谅无有，苜蓿聊可嚼。<div id='poem_sentence_13_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_520343'>况闻豆积岭，中有不死药。<div id='poem_sentence_14_520343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_520343'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_520343_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
凤县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d67d9f7cfab94a5780da5896e161c072_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d67d9f7cfab94a5780da5896e161c072");'><span id='d67d9f7cfab94a5780da5896e161c072_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1107')">1105-1107年</a>，35-37岁</div><div id='d67d9f7cfab94a5780da5896e161c072' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　在凤州任州学教授，有文。作品：《送苗师彦序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称唐庚是年秋仍在绵州任上，有文《绵州谢监司举辟启》，后除凤州教授，与黄鹏所记异，黄鹏并未提及绵州任事，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_1213120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苗师颜序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213120")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213120'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213120'>崇宁元年冬，兴元军士有怨其守费诜者，走益昌上变告诜叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213120_comment'></div>益昌守得之惶惑，夜半遣吏驰出城，趋兴元捕反虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213120_comment'></div>即日以事闻，传檄郡国，拘其亲属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213120_comment'></div>后旬日，诜面缚至，并就逮者数十人，悉幪首系狱，穷治反状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213120_comment'></div>自冬迄夏，累月无所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213120_comment'></div>首鼠不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213120_comment'></div>朝廷疑之，迁其狱于凤翔，而天兴宰苗君师颜实领其事，时二年六月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213120_comment'></div>诜既槛就道，所至发卒鸣鼓，围绕护送，人皆意诜不能自白，而诜亦自度必死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213120_comment'></div>暨至岐下，一问而得实，八日而狱具，诜无毫发罪，即日破械出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213120_comment'></div>告者用赦窜海外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213120_comment'></div>诜之出也，感慨悲泣，观者顾指欢呼，道路相传，一日万口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213120_comment'></div>而师颜之名，遂满天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213120_comment'></div>吾尝论诜之不死，其所系岂小哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213120_comment'></div>向使一夫流言，二千石族诛以死，则士大夫必将姑息吏卒，谁敢控制？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213120_comment'></div>而使令厮役，皆得以胁制其主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213120_comment'></div>非朝廷之明白，师颜之俊伟，则搢绅之祸，岂独诜而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213120_comment'></div>汉时治狱，必取通经术、知古谊者，不可谓无意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213120_comment'></div>后二年，予官凤翔，师颜为治中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213120_comment'></div>得从之游，每服其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213120_comment'></div>而兴元之事，昔尝欲作传而未果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213120_comment'></div>于其归也，因以为之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1213120_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　秦陇间名医李生请序，庚为其方书作序。作品：《李生方书序》<div id='poem_1213127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李生方书序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213127")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213127'>《周官》硩蔟氏掌覆夭鸟之巢，庭氏掌射国中之大鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213127_comment'></div>吾少时读书至此，未尝不窃笑，以为不急之务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213127_comment'></div>后读《圣惠方》言：「有鸟夜飞，谓之『无辜』，小儿衣服遭之，辄以感疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213127_comment'></div>因以『无辜』言之，状如五疳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213127_comment'></div>吾以是知夭鸟之害有如此者，非独如郑氏所谓鸮鵩之类，而昔人所以力去者，亦自有旨，非独如郑氏所谓国中洁清而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213127_comment'></div>夫硩蔟氏、庭氏之所去者，虽不专指「无辜」，而「无辜」之出于斯时者，亦无所容其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213127_comment'></div>虽未必能尽诛，要当驱而出之于九州四海之外，而不得以为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213127_comment'></div>斯周公所建置，果不可谓不切于事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213127_comment'></div>周道衰，二官之职废，物之神奸遂得以滋息涵养于天地之内，数千百年，愈久而愈不可去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213127_comment'></div>故夭鸟之巢，往往有之，而世终莫之识，虽识亦无如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213127_comment'></div>当此之时，李生以善医「无辜」专门名家于秦陇间，其功利岂小哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213127_comment'></div>生出论数十篇示余，而求文以为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213127_comment'></div>吾闻扁鹊入秦为小儿医，生岂得其书乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213127_comment'></div>何其术之妙也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213127_comment'></div>年月日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1213127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　在凤州任州学教授，读苏辙《巢谷传》有感，作文批党禁。作品：《读巢元修撰》<div id='poem_1213129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读巢元脩传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213129")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213129'>唐末有郑遨者，与李振厚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213129_comment'></div>振仕梁至崇政使，遨未尝一至其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213129_comment'></div>后唐同光初，振窜岭外，遨徒步万里往见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213129_comment'></div>其后一百八十年，而宋有巢元脩事，士之难得盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213129_comment'></div>吾闻子由立朝，謇謇有大体，然靳惜名器太甚，良以是失士心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213129_comment'></div>比其败也，士大夫诋之又过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213129_comment'></div>观其书巢元脩事，可胜叹哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213129_comment'></div>可胜叹哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1213129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年五月</a>　朝廷班《纪元历》，上谢表。作品：《谢历日表》<div id='poem_1213069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢历日表<span class='inlineComment2'>（代翟提刑）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213069")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213069'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213069'>四时既宅，然后允釐于百工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213069_comment'></div>七政已齐，可以肆类于上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213069_comment'></div>盖析因夷隩之本，寔财成辅相之原<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213069_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下贲饰观天，革孚治历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213069_comment'></div>俾岁月日时无易，故金木土谷惟修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213069_comment'></div>臣承乏外台，复瞻新岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213069_comment'></div>日惟不足，岂小善之不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213069_comment'></div>时不再来，嗟大恩之未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213069_comment'></div>誓图寸效，不费分阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213069_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1213069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年五月二十一日</a>　长兄卒于丹稜，子唐文若生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年年初</a>　凤州州学教授任上，有文。作品：《上邓左丞书》<div id='poem_1213083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上邓左丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1107年年初）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213083")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213083'>尚书左丞阁下：某学术空虚，不能尽知前世事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213083_comment'></div>自建隆以来，数之蜀之先进，仕至两府者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213083_comment'></div>其行藏出处，是非长短，非后进小子所得轻议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213083_comment'></div>然大抵畏避形迹，不敢援引蜀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213083_comment'></div>盖起远方，孤立无与，过于虑患，不得不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213083_comment'></div>天圣中，阆人陈鸿渐以文章知名于世，制策入等，以季父当轴，不得召试，摈弃流落，饮恨至死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213083_comment'></div>引嫌之风，其由来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213083_comment'></div>自阁下执政，不复沿袭前事，每见蜀人，未尝不访问人物，虽不以天下名器私于蜀人，而蜀人之善，未有弃而不录者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213083_comment'></div>老成宿德，后生晚学，随宜录用，各当其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213083_comment'></div>至于甚愚无知如某等辈，犹得备员学校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213083_comment'></div>阁下既不自疑，而天下之人亦不以为私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213083_comment'></div>何其自任之重，自信之笃也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213083_comment'></div>某绍圣元年自太学归，从事州县，三任于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213083_comment'></div>勤苦于簿书狱讼而不以为劳，奔走于车尘马足而不以为卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213083_comment'></div>十年之间，遂无一字入国门者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213083_comment'></div>意谓古之为贫而仕，止当如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213083_comment'></div>既无以取知于人，遂不敢求于人知，而人亦无有知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213083_comment'></div>不知阁下得之于谁，遽有荐引，得非过于采听，而好事者遂得以欺左右乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213083_comment'></div>不然，何缘记忆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213083_comment'></div>某自到此，忽忽岁馀，事稍閒，不废读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213083_comment'></div>俸入差厚，足以为养，比之辈流，最为侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213083_comment'></div>所不满者，势有不便耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213083_comment'></div>风土气候非所宜，而饮食医药多不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213083_comment'></div>此其所以戚戚思蜀，而辄布腹心于受恩之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213083_comment'></div>古语有之：「为浮屠者，必合其尖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213083_comment'></div>此言虽小，亦自有理，惟阁下留意焉<span class='inlineComment2'>（《唐先生文集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213083_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1213083'>进：原阙，据四部丛刊本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1213083_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
常德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='768d3770dfa2432e9510751c3b718b88_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("768d3770dfa2432e9510751c3b718b88");'><span id='768d3770dfa2432e9510751c3b718b88_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>，40岁</div><div id='768d3770dfa2432e9510751c3b718b88' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　南迁途中，作诗记其行。作品：《武陵道中》<div id='poem_520170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>武陵道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520170")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520170'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520170'>朝持汉使节，暮作楚囚奔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520170'>路入离骚国，江通欸乃村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520170'>垣墙知地湿，草木验冬温。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520170'>寂寞桃源路，行人祗断魂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520170'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520170_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ed2834ed02849bd8d5098af05b11c13_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ed2834ed02849bd8d5098af05b11c13");'><span id='4ed2834ed02849bd8d5098af05b11c13_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>，40岁</div><div id='4ed2834ed02849bd8d5098af05b11c13' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　南迁途中，作诗记其行。作品：《长沙道中》<div id='poem_520171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长沙道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520171")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520171'>古古今今路，朝朝暮暮行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520171'>橘林香处饭，杉木翠边程。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520171'>山带湘灵惨，川含楚些清。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520171'>江湖无限句，迁客要才情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520171_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
