-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1fa4eb225ced4e909570b5d2b4130365_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fa4eb225ced4e909570b5d2b4130365");'><span id='1fa4eb225ced4e909570b5d2b4130365_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>，41岁</div><div id='1fa4eb225ced4e909570b5d2b4130365' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年正月初五</a>　南迁惠州，道出番禹，游越王台，有文记之。作品：《游越王台记》<div id='poem_1213150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游越王台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和元年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213150")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213150'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213150'>政和元年春，吾南迁惠州，道出番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213150_comment'></div>明日与客游越王台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213150_comment'></div>台据北山，其高数百寻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213150_comment'></div>南临小海，而潢溪、横浦、牂柯之水，辐辏于其下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213150_comment'></div>左右瞻顾，则越中诸山，不召而自至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213150_comment'></div>却立延望，则海外诸国，盖可仿佛于溟濛杳霭之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213150_comment'></div>吾游天下多矣，登临之胜，未有先于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213150_comment'></div>此其所以岿然千载，虽废而不毁也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213150_comment'></div>世言此台兴于汉初，废于元鼎之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213150_comment'></div>以吾观之，不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213150_comment'></div>昔樗里子之葬渭南也，曰：「后百年当有天子宫夹吾墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213150_comment'></div>至汉兴，长乐宫在其东，未央宫在其西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213150_comment'></div>谨按《史记》，秦昭王七年，岁在辛酉，樗里子卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213150_comment'></div>汉高帝七年，长乐宫成，八年营未央宫，是岁癸卯，上距辛酉实一百有三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213150_comment'></div>世知二宫作于高帝之时，而不知百年之前，樗里子固已言之于秦昭王之世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213150_comment'></div>古称得道至人，能知城邑宫殿从何福业生，此非虚语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213150_comment'></div>凡物成就，本非一时之所能为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213150_comment'></div>至其变灭，亦非一时之能废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213150_comment'></div>业凝而成，既泮而败，其所由来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213150_comment'></div>世无至人，故莫识其所从也，若樗里子者，岂足名得道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213150_comment'></div>彼不过以数知之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213150_comment'></div>盖万物本于道，故道能知之，不外于数，故数亦能知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213150_comment'></div>战国之士，大抵皆深于数，故知来事如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213150_comment'></div>至诘其所从来，彼亦不能言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213150_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213150_comment'></div>物之废兴妙矣，吾何足以知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213150_comment'></div>然于废兴之理，则吾尝论之孰矣，岂偶然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213150_comment'></div>至如士之所以成败得丧，彼亦有自来矣，岂云云者所能权之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213150_comment'></div>正月初五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1213150_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　游番禹县北越秀山悟性寺，作诗记之。作品：《游广州悟性寺，有赵王台，盖尉佗时所筑。有井，甘甚，号达摩井云》<div id='poem_520217' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520217?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游广州悟性寺寺有赵王台盖尉佗时所筑有井甘甚号达摩井云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520217")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520217_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520217'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520217'>崎岖走上方，浩荡取秋光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520217'>台上经樛女，江天入夜郎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520217'>华夷凭槛远，兴废引杯长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520217'>泉脉来何处，中含定慧香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520217'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520217_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dc798574d46548ae9ed344de089f7201_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dc798574d46548ae9ed344de089f7201");'><span id='dc798574d46548ae9ed344de089f7201_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>，45岁</div><div id='dc798574d46548ae9ed344de089f7201' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　北归至广州，作诗寄惠州故人。作品：《北归至广州寄惠州故人陈伯修、李文辅、梁德昭》<div id='poem_520167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北归至广州寄惠州故人<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈伯修、李文辅、梁昭德）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520167")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520167'>归心如跃马，奋迅不可驻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520167'>别情如故猿，已去犹返顾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520167'>三年孺子社，数借柱史书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520167'>好在五噫孙，善保千金躯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520167'>旧来谈天口，老去尽地力。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520167'>万里不相忘，寄声问眠食<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《唐先生文集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_520167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年十月初三</a>　次番禹，女儿船娘生。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
惠州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1033508b278241f38a8ba42982bfb0b1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1033508b278241f38a8ba42982bfb0b1");'><span id='1033508b278241f38a8ba42982bfb0b1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1115')">1111-1115年</a>，41-45岁</div><div id='1033508b278241f38a8ba42982bfb0b1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年正月</a>　至惠州，寓居郡城南沙子步李氏山园，有反思贬谪之作。作品：《李氏山园记》<div id='poem_1213157' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李氏山园记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213157")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213157_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213157'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213157'>伯阳甫续《史记》，后三百年而老聃伯阳为柱下史，后世因以伯阳甫为伯阳，则二人为一人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213157_comment'></div>范武子，晋士会也，而《古今人表》置士会于中上，列范武子于上中，则一人为二人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213157_comment'></div>岂惟人哉，龙目一名益智，而益智非龙目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213157_comment'></div>龙目出海南山谷间，味甘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213157_comment'></div>益智出西域，味辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213157_comment'></div>而《广雅》曰：「益智，龙目也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213157_comment'></div>则二物为一物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213157_comment'></div>枇杷、卢橘，一也，而《上林赋》曰：「卢橘夏熟，黄甘橙楱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213157_comment'></div>枇杷橪柿，亭奈厚朴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213157_comment'></div>则一物为二物矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213157_comment'></div>夫父祖之事，子孙有不及知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213157_comment'></div>州里之物，耆旧有不遍睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213157_comment'></div>而况述千载之上，数千万里之外者乎，亦何能无失耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213157_comment'></div>吾南迁惠州，寓居城南李氏之山园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213157_comment'></div>园高下数十亩，草木华实，无所不有，而龙目、卢橘为特盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213157_comment'></div>吾兄弟甥舅，无日不往来逍遥于其下，而笑旧说之谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213157_comment'></div>盖尝以比伯阳甫、范武子之事，而为之叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213157_comment'></div>因书其事，使后世知有是园，又知吾尝游戏于此，又知著述不可以不慎，而学诸子百家之言者，亦知其有得有失，而审所取云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1213157_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　谪居惠州，为斋作记。作品：《寄傲斋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（庐曰寄傲，庵曰易。）</span><div id='poem_1213154' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213154' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213154?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄傲斋记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213154")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213154_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213154'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213154'>吾谪居惠州，扫一室于所居之南，号「寄傲斋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213154_comment'></div>客指而笑曰：「此非取陶渊明之语乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213154_comment'></div>子居京师时，何尝念渊明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213154_comment'></div>能念渊明，当不至斥逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213154_comment'></div>今既至此，然后区区掇寄傲之语，以名其所居而见意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213154_comment'></div>晚矣，无及也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213154_comment'></div>吾愧谢曰：子责我是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213154_comment'></div>然岂知吾之心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213154_comment'></div>吾官阆中时，尝考论晋宋人物，至《渊明传》，慨然有感于吾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213154_comment'></div>时年三十，便有「归欤」之兴，求田问舍，亲友皆怪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213154_comment'></div>自是以来，俛仰十年，虽未即去，然田园之乐，未尝一日不系于心，而《归去来词》未尝一日不讽于口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213154_comment'></div>顷任博士，自以出处既不与隆替对，而迂愚拙直，又不能从英俊游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213154_comment'></div>数恳丞相，求西南一官以归，盖将老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213154_comment'></div>会奇祸作，以故不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213154_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213154_comment'></div>吾志不就，类皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213154_comment'></div>今虽云云，谁复信者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213154_comment'></div>信与不信，此复何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213154_comment'></div>顾惟鬼神知吾此心尔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213154_comment'></div>虽然，吾今适四十尔，天死吾于此乎，复何言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213154_comment'></div>设不吾死，得脱谪籍以归，则吾将以三十年之身，穷渊明之乐圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213154_comment'></div>吾名之以日涉之园门，吾名之以常关之扉林，吾名之以欣欣之林谷，吾名之以涓涓之谷壑，吾名之以窈窕之壑丘，吾名之以崎岖之丘，岂特取「寄傲」之语名一室而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213154_comment'></div>惟诗不近渊明，虽近亦不敢作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213154_comment'></div>独得其读书饮酒之趣，亦足以了一生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213154_comment'></div>收之桑榆，犹足以补东隅之失也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1213154_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1213154'><span class='label'>《传》不云乎：</span>「人之所欲，天必从之。」古人岂欺我哉？年月日记。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1213154_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　作诗自宽。作品：《初到惠州》<div id='poem_520175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初到惠州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520175")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520175'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520175'>卢橘杨梅乃尔甜，肯容迁谪到眉尖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520175'>因行采药非无得，取足看山未害廉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520175'>辨谤若为家一喙，著书不直字三缣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520175'>老师补处吾何敢，政为宗风不敢谦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520175'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520175_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年六月</a>　作文自嘲。作品：《省愆赋》<div id='poem_1213060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省愆赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213060")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213060'>唐子谪居岭表，既已半载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213060_comment'></div>杜门时省愆而慨曰：「身邪心邪，孰陷吾于罪乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213060_comment'></div>吾将求之身，则身非我有，四大所会，地水火风，谁为之宰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213060_comment'></div>吾将求之心，则心不在内，复不在外，不在中间，是将安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213060_comment'></div>昼夜以思，寝食皆废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213060_comment'></div>骨为之出，发为之改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213060_comment'></div>梦有告余曰：「甚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213060_comment'></div>子之蔽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213060_comment'></div>罪性本空，念念灭坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213060_comment'></div>反复寻绎，祗益咎悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213060_comment'></div>道逢臭腐，何足眄睐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213060_comment'></div>玩味不已，适足自秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213060_comment'></div>净是妄而况垢，谷犹无而矧稗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213060_comment'></div>譬之身体，本自安泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213060_comment'></div>或作病想，便若婴瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213060_comment'></div>识此病之谁受，尚何施于砭艾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213060_comment'></div>譬之手足，伸缩无碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213060_comment'></div>忽作缚想，举动辄絓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213060_comment'></div>悟此缚之无实，即无绳而可解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213060_comment'></div>方耸听于妙语，失胸中之结块。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213060_comment'></div>若春动而冰坼，若秋至而叶败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213060_comment'></div>回视无始以来，几千万世所作罪业，悉消散而崩溃矣，岂独今之所以流落颠沛者哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213060_comment'></div>觉而思之曰：「噫，此殆维摩诘也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213060_comment'></div>揽衣而起，正冠束带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213060_comment'></div>稽首西望，作礼而退。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1213060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　游丰湖，过东坡助筑之西新桥，欣然有所得，名曰“益桥”，作铭。作品：《益桥铭》<div id='poem_1213170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益桥铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213170")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213170'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213170'>吾闻九卦，主困而言也，而曰「益以兴利」者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213170_comment'></div>以为自利耶，则非所以为德之裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213170_comment'></div>以为利物耶，则非所以安困之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213170_comment'></div>数以问《易》师，《易》师皆不领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213170_comment'></div>政和元年，谪居鹅城，以暇日游丰湖，偃仰于桥亭之上，阅其款识，欣然而笑曰：「吾得之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213170_comment'></div>君子之心，何尝不欲兼济，而有所谓独善者，彼非得已也，顾力不足耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213170_comment'></div>方其不得已之时，而适有毫发便利可以益人，则虽穷厄九死之馀，苟可以致力，彼未有弃而不为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213170_comment'></div>都无可为矣，犹思所以为利于后代，而况于当世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213170_comment'></div>吾将得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213170_comment'></div>因名之曰「益桥」，而为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1213170'>过晋而悲，至燕而微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213170_comment'></div>一至之情，已过则移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213170_comment'></div>真悲不移，生死由是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213170_comment'></div>云何能然，有本所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213170_comment'></div>吾观此桥，日度万屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213170_comment'></div>积而计之，巧历莫数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213170_comment'></div>以穷苦时，作利济事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213170_comment'></div>乃知困中，有益之义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1213170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　登栖禅山，观东坡所言佛迹，有诗。作品：《登栖禅山》<div id='poem_520178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登栖禅山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520178")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_520178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520178'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520178'>海雨山烟拨不开，眼前遮定<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作尽）</span>望乡台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520178'>如何借得维摩手，断取西南故国来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520178'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_520178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年冬</a>　作诗记是年粮食丰收事。作品：《大熟行》<div id='poem_520152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大熟行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520152")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520152'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520152'>去年大雪埋尺箠，水北荔枝遭冻死。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520152'>共嗔北客带寒来，我欲分疏谁受理。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520152'>今年诸峒十分熟，东江不下龙川米<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作水）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520152'>南翁北客两欣然，孰与忍饥餐荔子。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520152_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520152'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年三月六日</a>　与友人于贬所寄傲斋斗茶，作文记之。作品：《斗茶记》<div id='poem_1213155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>斗茶记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年三月六日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213155")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213155'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213155'>政和二年三月壬戌，二三君子相与斗茶于寄傲斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213155_comment'></div>予为取龙塘水烹之，而第其品，以某为上，某次之，某闽人其所赍，宜尤高而又次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213155_comment'></div>然大较皆精绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213155_comment'></div>盖尝以为天下之物，有宜得而不得，不宜得而得之者，富贵有力之人或有所不能致，而贫贱穷厄、流离迁徙之中，或偶然获焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213155_comment'></div>所谓「尺有所短，寸有所长」，良不虚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213155_comment'></div>唐相李卫公好饮惠山泉，置驿传送，不远数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213155_comment'></div>而近世欧阳少师作《龙茶录序》，称嘉祐七年亲享明堂，致斋之夕，始以小团分赐二府，人给一饼，不敢碾试，至今藏之，时熙宁元年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213155_comment'></div>吾闻茶不问团銙，要之贵新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213155_comment'></div>水不问江井，要之贵活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213155_comment'></div>千里致水，真伪固不可知，就令识真，已非活水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213155_comment'></div>自嘉祐七年壬寅至熙宁元年戊申，首尾七年，更阅三朝，而赐茶犹在，此岂复有茶也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213155_comment'></div>今吾提瓶，走龙塘无数十步，此水宜茶，昔人以为不减清远峡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213155_comment'></div>而海道趋建安，不数日可至，故每岁新茶，不过三月至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213155_comment'></div>罪戾之馀，上宽不诛，得与诸公从容谈笑于此，汲泉煮茗，取一时之适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213155_comment'></div>虽在田野，孰与烹数千里之泉，浇七年之赐茗也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213155_comment'></div>此非吾君之力欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213155_comment'></div>夫耕凿食息，终日蒙福，而不知为之者，直愚民尔，岂我辈谓耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213155_comment'></div>是宜有所纪述，以无忘在上者之泽云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1213155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　惊闻张商英出知河南府，慨而作诗。作品：《有所叹二首》<div id='poem_520186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有所叹二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520186")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520186'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520186'>林中晏坐老沙门，岂愿临<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作频）</span>年触垢氛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520186'>正恐先生不得饱，欲令后死与斯文。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520186'>近逃台鼎居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_520186", 520186, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>东洛</span>，闻道衣冠满北军。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520186'>须信此涂天一握，人间漫说有孤云。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520186_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520186'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520186_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_520187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520187?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520187'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520187'>耕田佩印两徒然，忆相平津只去年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520187'>杯酌岂能通大道，床头当得酒如泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520187_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　作诗记饮食差劣。作品：《白小》<div id='poem_520156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_520156'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520156'>二年遵海滨，开眼即浩淼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年十月</a>　作诗记奇怪物候。作品：《十月复暄》<div id='poem_520194' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520194' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520194?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十月复暄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520194")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520194_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520194'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520194'>谁会世间事，即今冬后秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520194_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520194'>残年仍御袷，先日已重裘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520194_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520194'>地势炎州令，天时北客愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520194_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520194'>此生橐籥内，反复任吹咻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520194_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　谪居惠州，幼子蜑生，为作诗。作品：《示蜑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（幼子蜑为侍女黎氏生。）</span><div id='poem_520158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>示蜑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520158")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520158'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520158'>先君捐馆年，六十畸三算。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520158'>我今四十三，始得幼子蜑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520158'>馀龄继前躅，蜑也才及冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520158'>况复未可知，孝章积忧叹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520158'>禄养岂不欲，兹事觉已缓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520158'>但爱眉目秀，体质净如盥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520158'>顾瞻既精神，怀抱亦气岸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_520158'>今者新剔发，莹若珠未贯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_520158'>见之令人清，面拥疲手腕。<div id='poem_sentence_9_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_520158'>岂惟不肯嗔，更付一笑粲。<div id='poem_sentence_10_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_520158'>骨肉今远矣，恃汝慰奔窜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_520158'>行当从诸兄，诵书喧里闬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_520158'>而我于经术，粗能分句断。<div id='poem_sentence_13_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_520158'>发蒙要师资，心孔为开钻<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作关键）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_520158'>许慎专偏傍，张华休<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作谈）</span>史汉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_520158'>吾家业儒久，舍此无别段。<div id='poem_sentence_16_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_520158'>不应缘一噎，便欲废炊爨。<div id='poem_sentence_17_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_520158'>及亲三釜足，未用万户酂。<div id='poem_sentence_18_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_520158'>人生百年期，我今特未半。<div id='poem_sentence_19_520158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_520158'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_520158_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　作诗怀舍弟。作品：《夜坐怀舍弟》<div id='poem_520190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜坐怀舍弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_520190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520190'>沉陆伤吾道，浮生忆尔曹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520190_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_520188'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520188'>此日方收信，前时已具舟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520188'>开头今几<span class='inlineComment2'>（任本、汪本作岁）</span>月，软脚定中秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520188'>凉德为兄忝，炎荒代<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作为）</span>尔忧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520188_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　作诗思家人。作品：《鸣鹊行》<div id='poem_520159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鸣鹊行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520159")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520159'>檐前群鹊鸣相呼，法当有客或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_520159", 520159, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>远书</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520159'>吾今何处得书尺，而况宾客乘轩车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520159'>平生眼中抹泥涂，汎爱了不分贤愚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520159'>卒为所卖罪满躯，放逐南越烹蟾蜍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520159'>百口寄食西南隅，三年莫知安稳无。<div id='poem_sentence_4_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_520159'>家书已自不可必，更望故人双鲤鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_520159'>故人顷来绝能<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本作懒）</span>疏，况复万岭千江湖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_520159'>鸡肋曾是<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作足）</span>安拳馀，至今畏客如于菟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_520159'>岂惟避谤谢还往，此日谁肯窥吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_520159'>杜门却扫也不恶，何但忘客兼忘吾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_520159'>喧喧鸣鹊汝过矣，曷不往噪权门朱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_520159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_520159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_520159_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　作文志惠州风土。作品：《射象记》<div id='poem_1213156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213156?labeling=true' target='_blank'>射象记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213156")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213156_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213156'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213156'>政和三年三月乙卯，有象逸于惠州之北门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213156_comment'></div>惠人相与攻之，操戈戟、弓弩、火炬者，至数百人，而空手傍观，鼓噪以助勇者，亦以千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213156_comment'></div>既至，皆逡巡不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213156_comment'></div>有监税蒙顺国者，邕州边人，以趫捷自矜，短衣踊跃，挟数十矢射之，中项背如猬毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213156_comment'></div>象庞然不动，徐以鼻卷去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213156_comment'></div>最后中左耳，流血被面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213156_comment'></div>象怒驰之，顺国弃弓返走，未数步，象以鼻钩其膝，盘之于地，蹂践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213156_comment'></div>众溃散走，象亦缓缓引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213156_comment'></div>少焉，吏卒就视，则顺国已碎首折胁、陷胸流肠死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213156_comment'></div>吾时方食，闻之投箸叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213156_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213156_comment'></div>使象得入城，则鼻之所触，齿之所拂，足之所蹴，岂复有邑屋、居民、聚落也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213156_comment'></div>为万人排难，而以一身死之，此吾所以叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213156_comment'></div>然吾闻交趾捕象，必用机阱，未有直决者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213156_comment'></div>吾尝识其形矣，其立如屋，其卧如堤，其行如舟，是岂可与力竞也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213156_comment'></div>若人者，可谓愚矣，此吾所以又叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213156_comment'></div>然向使数百人者叶心勠力，齐奋而共击之，亦未必不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213156_comment'></div>脱令不胜，犹当不至于此，此吾所以又叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213156_comment'></div>虽然，古之不量事力，奋区区之忠，以排难救人为己任，而困于无助，以至碎首折胁、陷胸流肠而死者，亦安可胜数？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213156_comment'></div>凡有志而无成者，皆是也，何独此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213156_comment'></div>此吾所以又叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213156_comment'></div>作《射象记》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1213156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年三月</a>　作诗记物候。作品：《壬辰年九月不雨，至癸巳年三月，穑事去矣。今夕则沛然，喜甚。卧作此诗》（老去生涯白木镵）<div id='poem_520201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬辰九月不雨至<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪本下有癸字）</span>巳年三月穑事去矣今夕辄复霈然喜甚卧作此诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520201")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520201'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520201'>老去生涯白木镵，脱逢艰食更何堪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520201_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520201'>春深野色忧年恶，夜半檐声觉雨甘<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　与梅蟠游，有诗赠之。作品：《采药行赠梅蟠》<div id='poem_520160' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520160' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_520160'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520160_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年正月六日</a>　谪居惠州，有诗记与弟唐庾游西溪事。作品：《乙未正月丁丑，与舍弟棹小舟穷西溪至愁绝处，度不可进，乃归。溪侧有双榕，甚奇，清荫可庇数十榻，水东老人尝饮酒其下云》<div id='poem_520215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_3_520215'>应有居民解秦语，为言昭代好还乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520215'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年五月</a>　得到赦令北归之际，作诗示舍弟与外甥。作品：《有感示舍弟端孺并外甥郭圣俞》<div id='poem_520216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520216?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有感示舍弟端孺<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_0_520216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520216'>弟兄手足穷孤竹，母子肝肠泣老莱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520216'>好语忽从天上落，行人直向<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作叩）</span>海边回。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520216'>此生报国无他事，力穑供输莫待催。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520216'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520216_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年六月八日</a>　接复官承议郎表，上谢表。作品：《惠州谢复官表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（政和二年，宋朝改称官名，原宗学国子博士称承议郎。）</span><div id='poem_1213067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>惠州谢复官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年六月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213067")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213067'>臣某言：今月八日，惠州送到告身一道，伏蒙圣恩，复臣承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213067_comment'></div>臣已于当日祗受讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213067_comment'></div>始以为梦，既而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213067_comment'></div>俯伏拜恩，喑呜流涕<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213067_comment'></div>伏念臣生逢尧舜，迹虽涉于仕涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213067_comment'></div>性嗜老庄，口不谈于世事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213067_comment'></div>自知无用，非敢有求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213067_comment'></div>适遭学校之兴，累冒师儒之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213067_comment'></div>传经天姓，已负愧于面颜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213067_comment'></div>奉使日围，固难逃于指目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213067_comment'></div>果缘侥倖，卒至颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213067_comment'></div>命察如丝，罪几擢发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213067_comment'></div>奋空拳于岭表，不保朝昏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213067_comment'></div>托众口于江阳，莫知存没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213067_comment'></div>夷居万里，烟瘴六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213067_comment'></div>赖禀赋之冥顽，得保全于视息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213067_comment'></div>虽简编度日，益坚国尔之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213067_comment'></div>而兄弟灌园，已作家焉之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213067_comment'></div>岂期仕伍，复齿朝绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1213067_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下如日正中，惟天为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1213067_comment'></div>曰生曰杀，得驭臣之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1213067_comment'></div>作福作威，有惟辟之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1213067_comment'></div>建元良于震邸，均介福于坤舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1213067_comment'></div>旧恶宿愆，悉皆荡涤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1213067_comment'></div>前侯故将，咸被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1213067_comment'></div>而臣忧患摧伤，志意衰落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1213067_comment'></div>虽受再生之赐，终无一割之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1213067_comment'></div>唯作颂声，以歌圣治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1213067_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1213067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年六月二十四日</a>　接复官承议郎表，上谢庙记。作品：《水东庙记》<div id='poem_1213158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水东庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213158")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213158'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213158'>庙中神像二，其一介胄按剑而坐者曰兴祚王，其一乌巾紫襕、端笏而坐者曰泰民王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213158_comment'></div>观「兴祚」之名，疑南汉时所封，而不敢遂以为然者，盖无所考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213158_comment'></div>吾始至惠州，屏居于南山之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213158_comment'></div>北望西江之东，林木之间，夜夜有灯煜然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213158_comment'></div>里人曰：「此水东灵庙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213158_comment'></div>吾闻之竦然祷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213158_comment'></div>自是感于精神、发于梦寐者非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213158_comment'></div>以其事近怪，故不欲悉书，而要之灵应卓然，有不可不信者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213158_comment'></div>然吾尝闻之《易》矣，凡天道之所亏益，地道之所流变，鬼神之所祸福，与人之好恶，大抵相似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213158_comment'></div>吾今以无状不肖，获罪于世，至于中原之大，无所容其躯，而窜伏于五岭之南，罗浮之东，披黄茅而居者，五年而后归，则其见恶于人也，可谓极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213158_comment'></div>方是之时，虽吾之心，亦复自恶，而神独眷眷如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213158_comment'></div>意者鬼神之中，亦有异好者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213158_comment'></div>抑亦舍其迹而求其心，怜其穷厄而忘其罪戾，亦如吾君所以宽而不诛，已弃而复收之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213158_comment'></div>不然，何其与《易》相反？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213158_comment'></div>神之威德，始于神江，被于濒流数百里之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213158_comment'></div>故神江铁步、水东皆有庙，而水东庙为特盛，然皆不在祀典，故或者以为疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213158_comment'></div>夫以祀典而论鬼神，犹以阀阅而论人物也，便谓之尽可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213158_comment'></div>此亦无足疑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1213158_comment'></div>政和五年六月二十四日，眉山唐某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1213158_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　北归时，有诗。作品：《将赴阙，有感示聃》<div id='poem_520283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将赴阙有感示聃</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520283")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_520283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520283'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520283'>老畏高门地，慵便下泽车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520283'>终然婴世网，难作爱吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520283'>白平阳淫于，诗曹务尽废。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520283'>郡置假尉以，代之分其半。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520283_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520283'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年九月底</a>　离惠州。<br /></div>

沙市

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年五月</a>　北归至江陵，寓居沙头，幼女船娘夭，为作铭。作品：《船娘铭》<div id='poem_1213182' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213182' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213182?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舡娘铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和六年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213182'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213182'>舡娘，吾幼女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213182_comment'></div>政和五年，吾发惠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213182_comment'></div>次番禺，舣舟沧浪亭，而女于是乎生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213182_comment'></div>明年，至江陵，寓居于沙头，而女于是乎死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213182_comment'></div>是夕瘗于鹤鸣寺之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213182_comment'></div>其生也，以十月初三日，其死而瘗之也，以五月二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213182_comment'></div>凡居人世二百三十有三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213182_comment'></div>其将瘗也，其母黎氏持而哭之曰：「儿玉也，舍我安之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213182_comment'></div>吾即其语而为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213182_comment'></div>曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1213182'>空空如谷，何以得此玉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213182_comment'></div>终非作福，未几而毁于椟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1213182_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年五月</a>　郑居中为太宰，代人作贺启。作品：《贺郑太宰启》<div id='poem_1213092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺郑太宰启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213092")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213092'>伏审拜恩中陛，进位元台，凡在陶镕，实深庆抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213092_comment'></div>窃以虞刑未措，选于众而举皋陶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213092_comment'></div>商鼎将调，求诸野而得傅说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213092_comment'></div>备见载籍，号为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213092_comment'></div>然皋陶之术，非本于民情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213092_comment'></div>而傅说之举，不由于师锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213092_comment'></div>坐超迥古，允属圣时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213092_comment'></div>恭惟某官识照几先，学穷系表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213092_comment'></div>禁林视草，知盛德之有言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213092_comment'></div>枢极运筹，见真儒之无敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213092_comment'></div>既延登于揆路，实满慰于舆情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213092_comment'></div>以舜事尧，意其在此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213092_comment'></div>维申及甫，兹岂偶然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213092_comment'></div>必将尽摅胸臆之奇，庶几大慰迩遐之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213092_comment'></div>某侧闻诞告，实副愿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213092_comment'></div>徒深贺厦之诚，阻与扫门之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213092_comment'></div>永怀欣豫，未易名言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1213092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年五月</a>　刘正夫为少宰，代人作贺启。作品：《贺刘少宰启》<div id='poem_1213093' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1213093' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1213093?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺刘少宰启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_1213093")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1213093_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1213093'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1213093'>伏审拜恩天陛，进位台躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1213093_comment'></div>凡在陶镕，举深抃蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1213093_comment'></div>窃以国家安治，何啻百年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1213093_comment'></div>宰相称呼，盖尝屡易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1213093_comment'></div>置平章于后省，冠仆射于南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1213093_comment'></div>犹袭唐馀，未皇周制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1213093_comment'></div>主上亲纡宸翰，追述先猷，作新二宰之名，永著一王之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1213093_comment'></div>自非智足以断国论，仁足以遂物宜，则何以上副旁求，进膺大用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1213093_comment'></div>恭惟某官才推人杰，学造天民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1213093_comment'></div>言不外于圣人，故常合稷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1213093_comment'></div>喻必根于经术，岂肯借秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1213093_comment'></div>登二府者曾未数年，裨万乘者盖非一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1213093_comment'></div>逮兹爰立，实副具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1213093_comment'></div>所谓萧也规而曹也随，周公左而召公右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1213093_comment'></div>年登可待，刑措为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1213093_comment'></div>方此投闲，闻之起立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1213093_comment'></div>阻远潭潭之府，莫趋两两之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1213093_comment'></div>欣跃之诚，实倍伦等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1213093_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年九月十日</a>　与张商英相伴泛舟东湖，有诗。作品：《重阳日后一日从无尽泛舟游处士台故诗人秦龟从所居》<span class='inlineComment2'>（张商英以《和韵》赠，诗云：“饮散肩舆乘皓月，烛笼何用两行纱。”）</span><div id='poem_520272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重阳后一日从无尽泛舟游处士台故诗人秦龟从所居</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年九月十日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520272")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520272'>皂河经雨水微沙，船帖台根日未斜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520272'>三径就荒悲白土，一樽相属对黄花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520272'>已将远眺收平楚，更遣清言到永嘉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520272'>要见仙翁头似漆，请看醉后落乌纱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520272'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　于江陵逢故人宋德粹，作诗酬之。作品：《江陵逢故人宋德粹自播守罢归南阳，以诗见贻，依韵和酬》<div id='poem_520273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江陵逢故人宋德粹自播守罢归南阳以诗见贻依韵和酬</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520273'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520273'>昔别方初节，相逢各素秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520273'>君归卧龙国，我脱堕鸢州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520273'>霜鬓含多事，尘容带倦游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
凤翔
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='592e5202d44d43beacf993318eadf328_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("592e5202d44d43beacf993318eadf328");'><span id='592e5202d44d43beacf993318eadf328_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，51岁</div><div id='592e5202d44d43beacf993318eadf328' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　年初，行至凤翔，大病几死，幸得痊愈。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='00dcccdee872442c883bfe1fcfe0231e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("00dcccdee872442c883bfe1fcfe0231e");'><span id='00dcccdee872442c883bfe1fcfe0231e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，51岁</div><div id='00dcccdee872442c883bfe1fcfe0231e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年六月</a>　至泸南，僦居安夷门外，上书张观文四篇。作品：《再上张观文书四幅》<br /></div>

-----title
枝城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='da825d17c5c242a4a7441cf386a6b3b1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da825d17c5c242a4a7441cf386a6b3b1");'><span id='da825d17c5c242a4a7441cf386a6b3b1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>，51岁</div><div id='da825d17c5c242a4a7441cf386a6b3b1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年春末夏初</a>　至宜都，逢李六，有诗。作品：《生还至宜都逢李六》<span class='inlineComment2'>（马德富《唐庚年谱》（《宋人年谱丛刊》第六册）称此诗作于政和七年，与黄鹏异，暂依黄鹏记录。）</span><div id='poem_520276' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_520276' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/520276?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生还至宜都逢李六</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年春末夏初）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24980, "北宋", "唐庚", "poem_title_520276")'>唐庚</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_520276_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_520276'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_520276'>更把馀年著酒浇，莫谈前事废灯挑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_520276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_520276'>地缘有语封还止，印为无功铸复销。<div id='poem_sentence_1_520276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_520276'>赖是诗书能却瘴，到今魂梦亦闻潮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_520276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_520276'>头西归去君休怪，尾段无多不奈焦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_520276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_520276'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_520276_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
